secret top of oreb or  sinai didst inspire that shepherd who first taught  chosen seed in  beginning how  heav’ns  earth rose out  chaos or if sion hill delight thee more  siloa’s brook  flow’d fast   oracle  god i thence invoke thy aid  my adventrous song that  no middle flight intends  soar above th’ aonian mount while  pursues things unattempted yet  prose or rhime and chiefly thou o spirit  dost prefer before all temples th’ upright heart  pure instruct me  thou know’st thou   first wast present   mighty wings outspread dovelike satst brooding   vast abyss and mad’st  pregnant what  me  dark illumine what  low raise  support that   highth  this great argument i may assert th’ eternal providence and justifie  wayes  god  men say first  heav’n hides nothing  thy view nor  deep tract  hell say first what cause mov’d our grand parents   happy state favour’d  heav’n so highly  fall off from their creator  transgress his will for one restraint lords   world besides who first seduc’d them   fowl revolt th’ infernal serpent   was whose guile stird up  envy  revenge deceiv’d the mother  mankinde what time his pride had cast him out  heav’n  all his host of rebel angels  whose aid aspiring to set himself  glory above his peers he trusted  have equal’d  most high if  oppos’d   ambitious aim against  throne  monarchy  god rais’d impious war  heav’n  battel proud with vain attempt him  almighty power hurld headlong flaming  th’ ethereal skie with hideous ruine  combustion down to bottomless perdition there  dwell in adamantine chains  penal fire who durst defie th’ omnipotent  arms nine times  space  measures day  night to mortal men   his horrid crew lay vanquisht rowling   fiery gulfe confounded though immortal but his doom reserv’d him  more wrath  now  thought both  lost happiness  lasting pain torments him round  throws his baleful eyes that witness’d huge affliction  dismay mixt  obdurate pride  stedfast hate at once  far  angels kenn  views the dismal situation waste  wilde a dungeon horrible  all sides round as one great furnace flam’d yet  those flames no light but rather darkness visible serv’d only  discover sights  woe regions  sorrow doleful shades where peace and rest can never dwell hope never comes that comes  all but torture without end still urges   fiery deluge fed with everburning sulphur unconsum’d such place eternal justice had prepar’d for those rebellious here their prison ordain’d in utter darkness  their portion set as far remov’d  god  light  heav’n as   center thrice  th’ utmost pole o how unlike  place  whence they fell there  companions  his fall o’rewhelm’d with floods  whirlwinds  tempestuous fire he soon discerns  weltring  his side one next himself  power  next  crime long after known  palestine  nam’d beelzebub to whom th’ archenemy and thence  heav’n call’d satan  bold words breaking  horrid silence thus began if thou beest he but o how fall’n how chang’d from him who   happy realms  light cloth’d  transcendent brightnes didst outshine myriads though bright if  whom mutual league united thoughts  counsels equal hope and hazard   glorious enterprize joynd  me once now misery hath joynd in equal ruin into what pit thou seest from what highth fal’n so much  stronger provd he  his thunder  till then who knew the force  those dire arms yet not  those nor what  potent victor  his rage can else inflict do i repent or change though chang’d  outward lustre  fixt mind and high disdain  sence  injur’d merit that   mightiest rais’d me  contend and   fierce contention brought along innumerable force  spirits arm’d that durst dislike his reign  me preferring his utmost power  adverse power oppos’d in dubious battel   plains  heav’n and shook his throne what though  field  lost all  not lost  unconquerable will and study  revenge immortal hate and courage never  submit or yield and what  else not   overcome that glory never shall his wrath or might extort  me to bow  sue  grace with suppliant knee  deifie his power who   terrour  this arm so late doubted his empire   low indeed that   ignominy  shame beneath this downfall since  fate  strength  gods and this empyreal substance cannot fail since through experience  this great event in arms not worse  foresight much advanc’t we may  more successful hope resolve to wage  force or guile eternal warr irreconcileable  our grand foe who now triumphs   th’ excess  joy sole reigning holds  tyranny  heav’n so spake th’ apostate angel though  pain vaunting aloud but rackt  deep despare and him thus answer’d soon his bold compeer o prince o chief  many throned powers that led th’ imbattelld seraphim  warr under thy conduct   dreadful deeds fearless endanger’d heav’ns perpetual king and put  proof his high supremacy whether upheld  strength or chance or fate too well i see  rue  dire event that  sad overthrow  foul defeat hath lost us heav’n  all this mighty host in horrible destruction laid thus low as far  gods  heav’nly essences can perish   mind  spirit remains invincible  vigour soon returns though all our glory extinct  happy state here swallow’d up  endless misery but what if  our conquerour whom i now of force believe almighty since no less then such could hav orepow’rd such force  ours have left us this our spirit  strength intire strongly  suffer  support our pains that we may so suffice his vengeful ire or do him mightier service  his thralls by right  warr what e’re his business  here   heart  hell  work  fire or do his errands   gloomy deep what can  then avail though yet we feel strength undiminisht or eternal being to undergo eternal punishment whereto  speedy words th’ archfiend reply’d fall’n cherube   weak  miserable doing or suffering but  this  sure to do ought good never   our task but ever  do ill our sole delight as being  contrary  his high  whom we resist if then his providence out  our evil seek  bring forth good our labour must   pervert  end and out  good still  find means  evil which oft times may succeed so  perhaps shall grieve him if i fail not  disturb his inmost counsels  their destind aim but see  angry victor hath recall’d his ministers  vengeance  pursuit back   gates  heav’n the sulphurous hail shot after us  storm oreblown hath laid the fiery surge    precipice of heav’n receiv’d us falling   thunder wing’d  red lightning  impetuous rage perhaps hath spent his shafts  ceases now to bellow through  vast  boundless deep let us not slip th’ occasion whether scorn or satiate fury yield   our foe seest thou yon dreary plain forlorn  wilde the seat  desolation voyd  light save what  glimmering  these livid flames casts pale  dreadful thither let us tend from off  tossing  these fiery waves there rest if any rest can harbour there and reassembling our afflicted powers consult how we may henceforth most offend our enemy our own loss how repair how overcome this dire calamity what reinforcement we may gain  hope if not what resolution  despare thus satan talking  his neerest mate with head uplift above  wave  eyes that sparkling blaz’d his other parts besides prone   flood extended long  large lay floating many  rood  bulk  huge as whom  fables name  monstrous size titanian or earthborn  warr’d  jove briarios or typhon whom  den by ancient tarsus held or  seabeast leviathan which god  all his works created hugest  swim th’ ocean stream him haply slumbring   norway foam the pilot  some small nightfounder’d skiff deeming some island oft  seamen tell with fixed anchor  his skaly rind moors  his side under  lee while night invests  sea  wished morn delayes so stretcht out huge  length  archfiend lay chain’d   burning lake nor ever thence had ris’n or heav’d his head but    and high permission  allruling heaven left him  large  his own dark designs that  reiterated crimes  might heap  himself damnation while  sought evil  others  enrag’d might see how all his malice serv’d but  bring forth infinite goodness grace  mercy shewn on man  him seduc’t but  himself treble confusion wrath  vengeance pour’d forthwith upright  rears  off  pool his mighty stature  each hand  flames drivn backward slope their pointing spires  rowld in billows leave i’th’ midst  horrid vale then  expanded wings  stears his flight aloft incumbent   dusky air that felt unusual weight till  dry land he lights if   land  ever burn’d with solid   lake  liquid fire and such appear’d  hue  when  force of subterranean wind transports  hill torn  pelorus or  shatter’d side of thundring aetna whose combustible and fewel’d entrals thence conceiving fire sublim’d  mineral fury aid  winds and leave  singed bottom all involv’d with stench  smoak such resting found  sole of unblest feet him followed his next mate both glorying  have scap’t  stygian flood as gods   their own recover’d strength not   sufferance  supernal power is this  region this  soil  clime said then  lost arch angel this  seat that we must change  heav’n this mournful gloom for  celestial light be  so since hee who now  sovran can dispose  bid what shall  right fardest  him  best whom reason hath equald force hath made supream above his equals farewel happy fields where joy  ever dwells hail horrours hail infernal world  thou profoundest hell receive thy new possessor one who brings a mind not   chang’d  place or time the mind   own place    self can make  heav’n  hell  hell  heav’n what matter where if i  still  same and what i should be all but less then hee whom thunder hath made greater here  least we shall  free th’ almighty hath not built here  his envy  not drive us hence here we may reign secure   my choyce to reign  worth ambition though  hell better  reign  hell then serve  heav’n but wherefore let we then our faithful friends th’ associates  copartners  our loss lye thus astonisht  th’ oblivious pool and call them not  share  us their part in this unhappy mansion or once more with rallied arms  try what may  yet regaind  heav’n or what more lost  hell so satan spake  him beelzebub thus answer’d leader  those armies bright which but th’ omnipotent none could have foyld if once they hear  voyce their liveliest pledge of hope  fears  dangers heard so oft in worst extreams    perilous edge of battel when  rag’d  all assaults their surest signal they  soon resume new courage  revive though now they lye groveling  prostrate  yon lake  fire as we erewhile astounded  amaz’d no wonder fall’n such  pernicious highth he scarce had ceas’t when  superiour fiend was moving toward  shore his ponderous shield ethereal temper massy large  round behind him cast  broad circumference hung  his shoulders like  moon whose orb through optic glass  tuscan artist views at ev’ning   top  fesole or  valdarno  descry new lands rivers or mountains  her spotty globe his spear  equal which  tallest pine hewn  norwegian hills    mast of some great ammiral  but  wand he walkt   support uneasie steps over  burning marle not like those steps on heavens azure   torrid clime smote  him sore besides vaulted  fire nathless  so endur’d till   beach of  inflamed sea  stood  call’d his legions angel forms who lay intrans’t thick  autumnal leaves  strow  brooks in vallombrosa where th’ etrurian shades high overarch’t imbowr or scatterd sedge afloat when  fierce winds orion arm’d hath vext  redsea coast whose waves orethrew busiris  his memphian chivalrie vvhile  perfidious hatred they pursu’d the sojourners  goshen who beheld from  safe shore their floating carkases and broken chariot wheels so thick bestrown abject  lost lay these covering  flood under amazement  their hideous change he call’d so loud  all  hollow deep of hell resounded princes potentates warriers  flowr  heav’n once yours now lost if such astonishment  this can sieze eternal spirits or have ye chos’n this place after  toyl  battel  repose your wearied vertue   ease you find to slumber here    vales  heav’n or  this abject posture have ye sworn to adore  conquerour who now beholds cherube  seraph rowling   flood with scatter’d arms  ensigns till anon his swift pursuers  heav’n gates discern th’ advantage  descending tread us down thus drooping or  linked thunderbolts transfix us   bottom  this gulfe awake arise or   ever fall’n they heard   abasht  up they sprung upon  wing  when men wont  watch on duty sleeping found  whom they dread rouse  bestir themselves ere well awake nor did they not perceave  evil plight in which they were or  fierce pains not feel yet  their generals voyce they soon obeyd innumerable as when  potent rod of amrams son  egypts evill day wav’d round  coast up call’d  pitchy cloud of locusts warping   eastern wind that ore  realm  impious pharoah hung like night  darken’d all  land  nile so numberless  those bad angels seen hovering  wing under  cope  hell ’twixt upper nether  surrounding fires till   signal giv’n th’ uplifted spear of their great sultan waving  direct thir course  even ballance down they light on  firm brimstone  fill all  plain a multitude like which  populous north pour’d never  her frozen loyns  pass rhene or  danaw when her barbarous sons came like  deluge   south  spread beneath gibraltar   lybian sands forthwith  every squadron  each band the heads  leaders thither hast where stood their great commander godlike shapes  forms excelling human princely dignities and powers  earst  heaven sat  thrones though  their names  heav’nly records now be no memorial blotted out  ras’d by thir rebellion   books  life nor had they yet among  sons  eve got them new names till wandring ore  earth through gods high sufferance   tryal  man by falsities  lyes  greatest part of mankind they corrupted  forsake god their creator  th’ invisible glory  him  made them  transform oft   image   brute adorn’d with gay religions full  pomp  gold and devils  adore  deities then  they known  men  various names and various idols through  heathen world say muse their names then known who first who last rous’d   slumber   fiery couch at thir great emperors call  next  worth came singly where  stood   bare strand while  promiscuous croud stood yet aloof the chief  those who   pit  hell roaming  seek their prey  earth durst fix their seats long after next  seat  god their altars  his altar gods ador’d among  nations round  durst abide jehovah thundring out  sion thron’d between  cherubim yea often plac’d within his sanctuary  self their shrines abominations   cursed things his holy rites  solemn feasts profan’d and  their darkness durst affront his light first moloch horrid king besmear’d  blood of human sacrifice  parents tears though   noyse  drums  timbrels loud their childrens cries unheard  past through fire to his grim idol him  ammonite worshipt  rabba  her watry plain in argob   basan   stream of utmost arnon nor content  such audacious neighbourhood  wisest heart of solomon  led  fraud  build his temple right against  temple  god on  opprobrious hill  made his grove the pleasant vally  hinnom tophet thence and black gehenna call’d  type  hell next chemos th’ obscene dread  moabs sons from aroer  nebo   wild of southmost abarim  hesebon and heronaim seons realm beyond the flowry dale  sibma clad  vines and eleale  th’ asphaltick pool peor his other name when  entic’d israel  sittim  their march  nile to do him wanton rites which cost them woe yet thence his lustful orgies  enlarg’d even   hill  scandal   grove of moloch homicide lust hard  hate till good josiah drove them thence  hell with these came they who   bordring flood of old euphrates   brook  parts egypt  syrian ground had general names of baalim  ashtaroth those male these feminine for spirits when they please can either sex assume or both so soft and uncompounded  their essence pure not ti’d or manacl’d  joynt or limb nor founded   brittle strength  bones like cumbrous flesh but  what shape they choose dilated or condens’t bright or obscure can execute their aerie purposes and works  love or enmity fulfill for those  race  israel oft forsook their living strength  unfrequented left his righteous altar bowing lowly down to bestial gods  which their heads  low bow’d down  battel sunk before  spear of despicable foes with these  troop came astoreth whom  phoenicians call’d astarte queen  heav’n  crescent horns to whose bright image nightly   moon sidonian virgins paid their vows  songs in sion also not unsung where stood her temple  th’ offensive mountain built by  uxorious king whose heart though large beguil’d  fair idolatresses fell to idols foul thammuz came next behind whose annual wound  lebanon allur’d the syrian damsels  lament his fate in amorous dittyes all  summers day while smooth adonis  his native rock ran purple   sea suppos’d  blood of thammuz yearly wounded  lovetale infected sions daughters  like heat whose wanton passions   sacred porch ezekiel saw when   vision led his eye survay’d  dark idolatries of alienated judah next came one who mourn’d  earnest when  captive ark maim’d his brute image head  hands lopt off in his own temple   grunsel edge where  fell flat  sham’d his worshipers dagon his name sea monster upward man and downward fish yet had his temple high rear’d  azotus dreaded through  coast of palestine  gath  ascalon and accaron  gaza’s frontier bounds him follow’d rimmon whose delightful seat was fair damscus   fertil banks of abbana  pharphar lucid streams he also against  house  god  bold a leper once  lost  gain’d  king ahaz his sottish conquerour whom  drew gods altar  disparage  displace for one  syrian mode whereon  burn his odious offrings  adore  gods whom  had vanquisht after these appear’d a crew who under names  old renown osiris isis orus  their train with monstrous shapes  sorceries abus’d fanatic egypt  her priests  seek thir wandring gods disguis’d  brutish forms rather then human nor did israel scape th’ infection when their borrow’d gold compos’d the calf  oreb   rebel king doubl’d  sin  bethel   dan lik’ning his maker   grazed ox jehovah who  one night when  pass’d from egypt marching equal’d  one stroke both her first born  all her bleating gods belial came last then whom  spirit more lewd fell not  heaven or more gross  love vice   self to him no temple stood or altar smoak’d yet who more oft then hee in temples   altars when  priest turns atheist  did ely’s sons who fill’d with lust  violence  house  god in courts  palaces  also reigns and  luxurious cities where  noyse of riot ascends above thir loftiest towrs and injury  outrage and when night darkens  streets then wander forth  sons of belial flown  insolence  wine witness  streets  sodom   night in gibeah when hospitable dores yielded thir matrons  prevent worse rape these   prime  order   might the rest  long  tell though far renown’d th’ ionian gods  javans issue held gods yet confest later then heav’n  earth thir boasted parents titan heav’ns first born with his enormous brood  birthright seis’d by younger saturn   mightier jove his own  rhea’s son like measure found so jove usurping reign’d these first  creet and ida known thence   snowy top of cold olympus rul’d  middle air thir highest heav’n or   delphian cliff or  dodona  through all  bounds of doric land or who  saturn old fled over adria  th’ hesperian fields and ore  celtic roam’d  utmost isles all these  more came flocking but  looks down cast  damp yet such wherein appear’d obscure som glimps  joy  have found thir chief not  despair  have found themselves not lost in loss  self which  his count’nance cast like doubtful hue but  his wonted pride soon recollecting  high words  bore semblance  worth not substance gently rais’d their fainted courage  dispel’d their fears then strait commands    warlike sound of trumpets loud  clarions  upreard his mighty standard  proud honour claim’d azazel  his right  cherube tall who forthwith   glittering staff unfurld th’ imperial ensign which full high advanc’t shon like  meteor streaming   wind with gemms  golden lustre rich imblaz’d seraphic arms  trophies all  while sonorous mettal blowing martial sounds at which  universal host upsent a shout  tore hells concave  beyond frighted  reign  chaos  old night all   moment through  gloom  seen ten thousand banners rise into  air with orient colours waving  them rose a forrest huge  spears  thronging helms appear’d  serried shields  thick array of depth immeasurable anon they move in perfect phalanx   dorian mood of flutes  soft recorders such  rais’d to highth  noblest temper hero’s old arming  battel   stead  rage deliberate valour breath’d firm  unmov’d with dread  death  flight or foul retreat nor wanting power  mitigate  swage with solemn touches troubl’d thoughts  chase anguish  doubt  fear  sorrow  pain from mortal or immortal minds thus they breathing united force  fixed thought mov’d   silence  soft pipes  charm’d thir painful steps o’re  burnt soyle  now advanc’t  view they stand  horrid front of dreadful length  dazling arms  guise of warriers old  order’d spear  shield awaiting what command thir mighty chief had  impose he through  armed files darts his experienc’t eye  soon traverse the whole battalion views thir order due thir visages  stature   gods thir number last  summs and now his heart distends  pride  hardning  his strength glories for never since created man met such imbodied force  nam’d  these could merit more then  small infantry warr’d   cranes though all  giant brood of phlegra  th’ heroic race  joyn’d that fought  theb’s  ilium  each side mixt  auxiliar gods  what resounds in fable or romance  uthers son begirt  british  armoric knights and all who since baptiz’d or infidel jousted  aspramont or montalban damasco or marocco or trebisond or whom biserta sent  afric shore when charlemain  all his peerage fell by fontarabbia thus far these beyond compare  mortal prowess yet observ’d thir dread commander  above  rest in shape  gesture proudly eminent stood like  towr his form had yet not lost all her original brightness nor appear’d less then arch angel ruind  th’ excess of glory obscur’d as when  sun new ris’n looks through  horizontal misty air shorn  his beams or  behind  moon in dim eclips disastrous twilight sheds on half  nations   fear  change perplexes monarchs dark’n’d so yet shon above them all th’ arch angel but his face deep scars  thunder had intrencht  care sat  his faded cheek but under browes of dauntless courage  considerate pride waiting revenge cruel his eye but cast signs  remorse  passion  behold the fellows  his crime  followers rather far other once beheld  bliss condemn’d for ever now  have their lot  pain millions  spirits  his fault amerc’t of heav’n   eternal splendors flung for his revolt yet faithfull how they stood thir glory witherd as when heavens fire hath scath’d  forrest oaks or mountain pines with singed top their stately growth though bare stands   blasted heath he now prepar’d to speak whereat their doubl’d ranks they bend from wing  wing  half enclose him round with all his peers attention held them mute thrice  assayd  thrice  spite  scorn tears such  angels weep burst forth  last words interwove  sighs found out their way o myriads  immortal spirits o powers matchless but  th’ almighty   strife was not inglorious though th’ event  dire as this place testifies  this dire change hateful  utter but what power  mind foreseeing or presaging   depth of knowledge past or present could have fear’d how such united force  gods how such as stood like these could ever know repulse for who can yet beleeve though after loss that all these puissant legions whose exile hath emptied heav’n shall faile  reascend selfrais’d  repossess their native seat for me  witness all  host  heav’n if counsels different or danger shun’d by me have lost our hopes but  who reigns monarch  heav’n till then  one secure sat  his throne upheld  old repute consent or custome  his regal state put forth  full but still his strength conceal’d which tempted our attempt  wrought our fall henceforth his might we know  know our own so  not either  provoke or dread new warr provok’t our better part remains to work  close design  fraud or guile what force effected not   no less at length  us may find who overcomes by force hath overcome but half his foe space may produce new worlds whereof so rife there went  fame  heav’n   ere long intended  create  therein plant a generation whom his choice regard should favour equal   sons  heaven thither if but  prie shall  perhaps our first eruption thither or elsewhere for this infernal pit shall never hold caelestial spirits  bondage nor th’ abysse long under darkness cover but these thoughts full counsel must mature peace  despaird for who can think submission warr then warr open or understood must  resolv’d he spake   confirm his words outflew millions  flaming swords drawn   thighs of mighty cherubim  sudden blaze far round illumin’d hell highly they rag’d against  highest  fierce  grasped arm’s clash’d  their sounding shields  din  war hurling defiance toward  vault  heav’n there stood  hill not far whose griesly top belch’d fire  rowling smoak  rest entire shon   glossie scurff undoubted sign that  his womb  hid metallic ore the work  sulphur thither wing’d  speed a numerous brigad hasten’d as when bands of pioners  spade  pickaxe arm’d forerun  royal camp  trench  field or cast  rampart mammon led them on mammon  least erected spirit  fell from heav’n  ev’n  heav’n his looks  thoughts were always downward bent admiring more the riches  heav’ns pavement trod’n gold then aught divine or holy else enjoy’d in vision beatific  him first men also   his suggestion taught ransack’d  center   impious hands rifl’d  bowels  thir mother earth for treasures better hid soon had his crew op’nd into  hill  spacious wound and dig’d out ribs  gold let none admire that riches grow  hell  soyle may best deserve  pretious bane and here let those who boast  mortal things  wondring tell of babel   works  memphian kings learn how thir greatest monuments  fame and strength  art  easily outdone by spirits reprobate    hour what   age they  incessant toyle and hands innumerable scarce perform nigh   plain  many cells prepar’d that underneath had veins  liquid fire sluc’d   lake  second multitude with wondrous art founded  massie ore severing each kinde  scum’d  bullion dross a third  soon had form’d within  ground a various mould    boyling cells by strange conveyance fill’d each hollow nook as   organ  one blast  wind to many  row  pipes  soundboard breaths anon out   earth  fabrick huge rose like  exhalation   sound of dulcet symphonies  voices sweet built like  temple where pilasters round were set  doric pillars overlaid with golden architrave nor did there want cornice or freeze  bossy sculptures grav’n the roof  fretted gold not babilon nor great alcairo such magnificence equal’d  all thir glories  inshrine belus or serapis thir gods or seat thir kings when aegypt  assyria strove in wealth  luxurie th’ ascending pile stood fixt her stately highth  strait  dores op’ning thir brazen foulds discover wide within her ample spaces o’re  smooth and level pavement   arched roof pendant  suttle magic many  row of starry lamps  blazing cressets fed with naphtha  asphaltus yeilded light as   sky the hasty multitude admiring enter’d   work some praise and some  architect his hand  known in heav’n  many  towred structure high where scepter’d angels held thir residence and sat  princes whom  supreme king exalted  such power  gave  rule each  his herarchie  orders bright nor  his name unheard or unador’d in ancient greece   ausonian land men call’d him mulciber  how  fell from heav’n they fabl’d thrown  angry jove sheer o’re  chrystal battlements  morn to noon  fell  noon  dewy eve a summers day    setting sun dropt   zenith like  falling star on lemnos th’ aegaean ile thus they relate erring    this rebellious rout fell long before nor aught avail’d him now to have built  heav’n high towrs nor did  scape by all his engins but  headlong sent with his industrious crew  build  hell mean while  winged haralds  command of sovran power  awful ceremony and trumpets sound throughout  host proclaim a solemn councel forthwith   held at pandaemonium  high capital of satan  his peers thir summons call’d from every  band squared regiment by place or choice  worthiest they anon with hundreds   thousands trooping came attended all access  throng’d  gates and porches wide but chief  spacious hall though like  cover’d field where champions bold wont ride  arm’d    soldans chair defi’d  best  panim chivalry to mortal combat or carreer  lance thick swarm’d both   ground    air brusht   hiss  russling wings as bees in spring time when  sun  taurus rides poure forth thir populous youth about  hive in clusters they among fresh dews  flowers flie   fro or   smoothed plank the suburb  thir strawbuilt cittadel new rub’d  baume expatiate  confer thir state affairs so thick  aerie crowd swarm’d   straitn’d till  signal giv’n behold  wonder they but now who seemd in bigness  surpass earths giant sons now less then smallest dwarfs  narrow room throng numberless like  pigmean race beyond  indian mount or faerie elves whose midnight revels   forrest side or fountain fome belated peasant sees or dreams  sees while over head  moon sits arbitress  neerer   earth wheels her pale course they  thir mirth  dance intent  jocond music charm his ear at once  joy  fear his heart rebounds thus incorporeal spirits  smallest forms reduc’d thir shapes immense    large though without number still amidst  hall of  infernal court but far within and  thir own dimensions like themselves the great seraphic lords  cherubim in close recess  secret conclave sat a thousand demygods  golden seat’s frequent  full after short silence then and summons read  great consult began the end of the first book paradise lost book ii high   throne  royal state which far outshon  wealth  ormus   ind or where  gorgeous east  richest hand showrs  her kings barbaric imaginations thus displaid powers  dominions deities  heav’n for since no deep within her gulf can hold immortal vigor though opprest  fall’n i give not heav’n  lost from this descent celestial vertues rising  appear more glorious  more dread then  no fall and trust themselves  fear no second fate mee though just right   fixt laws  heav’n did first create your leader next free choice with what besides  counsel or  fight hath bin achievd  merit yet this loss thus farr  least recover’d hath much more establisht   safe unenvied throne yeilded  full consent the happier state in heav’n which follows dignity might draw envy  each inferior but who here will envy whom  highest place exposes formost  stand against  thunderers aime your bulwark  condemns  greatest share of endless pain do i seem now  thine eye so foul once deemd so fair in heav’n when  th’ assembly   sight of all  seraphim  thee combin’d in bold conspiracy against heav’ns king all   sudden miserable pain surpris’d arm’d out  thy head i sprung amazement seis’d all th’ host  heav’n back they recoild affraid at first  call’d me sin    sign portentous held me but familiar grown i pleas’d   attractive graces won the most averse thee chiefly who full oft thy self  me thy perfect image viewing becam’st enamour’d  such joy thou took’st with me  secret  my womb conceiv’d a growing burden mean while warr arose and fields  fought  heav’n wherein remaind for what could else  our almighty foe cleer victory  our part loss  rout through all  empyrean down they fell driv’n headlong   pitch  heaven down into this deep    general fall i also  which time this powerful key into my hand  giv’n  charge  keep these gates  ever shut which none can pass without my op’ning pensive here i sat alone but long i sat not till my womb pregnant  thee  now excessive grown prodigious motion felt  rueful throes at last this odious offspring whom thou seest thine own begotten breaking violent way tore through my entrails   fear  pain distorted all my nether shape thus grew transform’d but  my inbred enemie forth issu’d brandishing his fatal dart made  destroy i fled  cry’d out death hell trembl’d   hideous name  sigh’d from all her caves  back resounded death i fled but  pursu’d though more  seems inflam’d  lust then rage  swifter far me overtook his mother all dismaid and  embraces forcible  foule ingendring  me   rape begot these yelling monsters   ceasless cry surround me  thou sawst hourly conceiv’d and hourly born  sorrow infinite to me  when they list into  womb that bred them they return  howle  gnaw my bowels their repast then bursting forth afresh  conscious terrours vex me round that rest or intermission none i find before mine eyes  opposition sits grim death my son  foe who sets them on and me his parent would full soon devour for want  other prey but   knows his end  mine involvd  knows  i should prove  bitter morsel  his bane when ever  shall be so fate pronounc’d but thou o father i forewarn thee shun his deadly arrow neither vainly hope to  invulnerable  those bright arms though temper’d heav’nly   mortal dint save  who reigns above none can resist she finish’d   suttle fiend his lore soon learnd now milder  thus answerd smooth dear daughter since thou claim’st me  thy sire and my fair son here showst me  dear pledge of dalliance had  thee  heav’n  joys then sweet now sad  mention through dire change befalln us unforeseen unthought of know i come no enemie but  set free from out this dark  dismal house  pain both him  thee  all  heav’nly host of spirits   our just pretenses and  concurring signs ere now created vast  round  place  bliss in  pourlieues  heav’n  therein plac’t a race  upstart creatures  supply perhaps our vacant room though more remov’d least heav’n surcharg’d  potent multitude might hap  move new broiles be this or aught then this more secret now design’d i haste to know  this once known shall soon return and bring ye   place where thou  death shall dwell  ease  up  down unseen wing silently  buxom air imbalm’d with odours there ye shall  fed  fill’d immeasurably all things shall  your prey he ceas’d  both seemd highly pleasd  death grinnd horrible  gastly smile  hear his famine should  fill’d  blest his mawe destin’d   good hour no less rejoyc’d his mother bad  thus bespake her sire the key  this infernal pit  due and  command  heav’ns allpowerful king i keep  him forbidden  unlock these adamantine gates against all force death ready stands  interpose his dart fearless   o’rematcht  living might but what ow i  his commands above who compasst round of mine own brood   my bowels feed thou art my father thou my author thou my being gav’st me whom should i obey but thee whom follow thou wilt bring me soon to  new world  light  bliss among the gods who live  ease where i shall reign at thy right hand voluptuous  beseems thy daughter  thy darling without end thus saying  her side  fatal key sad instrument  all our woe she took and towards  gate rouling her bestial train forthwith  huge porcullis high up drew which but her self not all  stygian powers could once have mov’d then   keyhole turns th’ intricate wards  every bolt  highth and time  place  lost where eldest night and chaos ancestors  nature hold eternal anarchie amidst  noise of endless warrs   confusion stand for hot cold moist  dry four champions fierce strive high arbiter chance governs all into this wilde abyss the womb  nature  perhaps her grave of neither sea nor shore nor air nor fire but all these  thir pregnant causes mixt confus’dly  which thus must ever fight unless th’ almighty maker them ordain his dark materials  create more worlds into this wilde abyss  warie fiend stood   brink  hell  look’d  while pondering his voyage  no narrow frith he had  cross nor  his eare less peal’d with noises loud  ruinous to compare great things  small then when bellona storms with all her battering engines bent  rase som capital city or less then if this as   cloudy chair ascending rides audacious but  seat soon failing meets a vast vacuitie all unawares fluttring his pennons vain plumb down  drops ten thousand fadom deep   this hour down had been sure  paradise dying put   weeds  dominic or  franciscan think  pass disguis’d they pass  planets seven  pass  fixt and  crystalline sphear whose ballance weighs the trepidation talkt   first mov’d and now saint peter  heav’ns wicket seems to wait them  his keys  now  foot of heav’ns ascent they lift thir feet when loe a violent cross wind  either coast blows them transverse ten thousand leagues awry into  devious air then might ye see cowles hoods  habits  thir wearers tost and flutterd into raggs then reliques beads indulgences dispenses pardons bulls the sport  winds all these upwhirld aloft fly o’re  backside   world farr off into  limbo large  broad since calld the paradise  fools  few unknown long after now unpeopl’d  untrod all this dark globe  fiend found   pass’d and long  wanderd till  last  gleame of dawning light turnd thitherward  haste his travell’d steps farr distant hee descries ascending  degrees magnificent up   wall  heaven  structure high at top whereof but farr more rich appeerd the work    kingly palace gate with frontispice  diamond  gold imbellisht thick  sparkling orient gemmes the portal shon inimitable  earth by model or  shading pencil drawn the stairs  such  whereon jacob saw angels ascending  descending bands of guardians bright when   esau fled to padanaram   field  luz dreaming  night under  open skie and waking cri’d this   gate  heav’n each stair mysteriously  meant nor stood there alwaies but drawn up  heav’n somtimes viewless  underneath  bright sea flow’d of jasper or  liquid pearle whereon who after came  earth sayling arriv’d wafted  angels or flew o’re  lake rapt   chariot drawn  fiery steeds the stairs  then let down whether  dare the fiend  easie ascent or aggravate his sad exclusion   dores  bliss direct against which op’nd  beneath just o’re  blissful seat  paradise a passage down  th’ earth  passage wide wider  farr then   aftertimes over mount sion and though   large over  promis’d land  god so dear by which  visit oft those happy tribes on high behests his angels   fro pass’d frequent  his eye  choice regard from paneas  fount  jordans flood to beersaba where  holy land borders  aegypt   arabian shoare so wide  op’ning seemd where bounds  set to darkness such  bound  ocean wave satan  hence now   lower stair that scal’d  steps  gold  heav’n gate looks down  wonder   sudden view of all this world  once as when  scout through dark  desart wayes  peril gone all night  last  break  chearful dawne obtains  brow  some highclimbing hill which  his eye discovers unaware the goodly prospect  some forein land firstseen or some renownd metropolis with glistering spires  pinnacles adornd which now  rising sun guilds  his beams such wonder seis’d though after heaven seen the spirit maligne but much more envy seis’d at sight  all this world beheld so faire round  surveys  well might where  stood so high above  circling canopie of nights extended shade  eastern point of libra   fleecie starr  bears andromeda farr off atlantick seas beyond th’ horizon then  pole  pole he views  bredth  without longer pause down right into  worlds first region throws his flight precipitant  windes  ease through  pure marble air his oblique way amongst innumerable starrs  shon stars distant but nigh hand seemd other worlds or other worlds they seemd or happy iles like those hesperian gardens fam’d  old fortunate fields  groves  flourie vales thrice happy iles but who dwelt happy there he stayd not  enquire above them all the golden sun  splendor likest heaven allur’d his eye thither his course  bends through  calm firmament but up or downe by center or eccentric hard  tell or longitude where  great luminarie alooff  vulgar constellations thick that  his lordly eye keep distance due dispenses light  farr they  they move thir starry dance  numbers  compute days months  years towards his allchearing lamp turn swift their various motions or  turnd by his magnetic beam  gently warms the univers   each inward part with gentle penetration though unseen shoots invisible vertue even   deep so wondrously  set his station bright there lands  fiend  spot like which perhaps astronomer   sun’s lucent orbe through his glaz’d optic tube yet never saw the place  found beyond expression bright compar’d  aught  earth medal or stone not all parts like but all alike informd with radiant light  glowing iron  fire if mettal part seemd gold part silver cleer if stone carbuncle most or chrysolite rubie or topaz   twelve  shon in aarons brestplate   stone besides imagind rather oft then elsewhere seen that stone or like   which here below philosophers  vain so long have sought in vain though  thir powerful art they binde volatil hermes  call up unbound in various shapes old proteus   sea draind through  limbec  his native forme what wonder then if fields  regions here breathe forth elixir pure  rivers run potable gold when  one vertuous touch th’ archchimic sun so farr  us remote produces  terrestrial humor mixt here   dark so many precious things of colour glorious  effect so rare here matter new  gaze  devil met undazl’d farr  wide his eye commands for sight no obstacle found here nor shade but all sunshine  when his beams  noon culminate  th’ aequator  they now shot upward still direct whence no way round shadow  body opaque can fall   aire no where so cleer sharp’nd his visual ray to objects distant farr whereby  soon saw within kenn  glorious angel stand the same whom john saw also   sun his back  turnd but not his brightness hid of beaming sunnie raies  golden tiar circl’d his head nor less his locks behind illustrious  his shoulders fledge  wings lay waving round  som great charge imploy’d hee seemd or fixt  cogitation deep glad   spirit impure  now  hope to find who might direct his wandring flight to paradise  happie seat  man his journies end  our beginning woe but first  casts  change his proper shape which else might work him danger or delay and now  stripling cherube  appeers not   prime yet such   his face youth smil’d celestial   every limb sutable grace diffus’d so well  feignd under  coronet his flowing haire in curles  either cheek plaid wings  wore of many  colourd plume sprinkl’d  gold his habit fit  speed succinct  held before his decent steps  silver wand he drew not nigh unheard  angel bright ere  drew nigh his radiant visage turnd admonisht  his eare  strait  known th’ archangel uriel one   seav’n who  gods presence neerest  his throne stand ready  command   his eyes that run through all  heav’ns or down  th’ earth bear his swift errands over moist  dry o’re sea  land him satan thus accostes uriel  thou  those seav’n spirits  stand in sight  god’s high throne gloriously bright the first art wont his great authentic  interpreter through highest heav’n  bring where all his sons thy embassie attend and here art likeliest  supream decree like honour  obtain   his eye to visit oft this new creation round unspeakable desire  see  know all these his wondrous works but chiefly man his chief delight  favour him  whom all these his works so wondrous  ordaind hath brought me   quires  cherubim alone thus wandring brightest seraph tell in which  all these shining orbes hath man his fixed seat or fixed seat hath none but all these shining orbes his choice  dwell that i may find him   secret gaze or open admiration him behold on whom  great creator hath bestowd worlds   whom hath all these graces powrd that both  him  all things   meet the universal maker we may praise who justly hath drivn out his rebell foes to deepest hell   repair  loss created this new happie race  men to serve him better wise  all his wayes so spake  false dissembler unperceivd for neither man nor angel can discern hypocrisie  only evil  walks invisible except  god alone by his permissive will through heav’n  earth and oft though wisdom wake suspicion sleeps at wisdoms gate   simplicitie resigns her charge while goodness thinks no ill where no ill seems which now  once beguil’d uriel though regent   sun  held the sharpest sighted spirit  all  heav’n who   fraudulent impostor foule in his uprightness answer thus returnd faire angel thy desire which tends  know the works  god thereby  glorifie the great workmaister leads  no excess that reaches blame but rather merits praise the more  seems excess  led thee hither from thy empyreal mansion thus alone to witness  thine eyes what some perhaps contented  report heare onely  heav’n for wonderful indeed  all his works pleasant  know  worthiest   all had  remembrance alwayes  delight but what created mind can comprehend thir number or  wisdom infinite that brought them forth but hid thir causes deep i saw when  his word  formless mass this worlds material mould came   heap confusion heard his voice  wilde uproar stood rul’d stood vast infinitude confin’d till  his second bidding darkness fled light shon  order  disorder sprung swift  thir several quarters hasted then the cumbrous elements earth flood aire fire and this ethereal quintessence  heav’n flew upward spirited  various forms that rowld orbicular  turnd  starrs numberless  thou seest  how they move each had his place appointed each his course the rest  circuit walles this universe look downward   globe whose hither side with light  hence though but reflected shines that place  earth  seat  man  light his day which else  th’ other hemisphere night would invade but there  neighbouring moon so call  opposite fair starr her aide timely interposes  her monthly round still ending still renewing through mid heav’n with borrowd light her countenance triform hence fills  empties  enlighten th’ earth and  her pale dominion checks  night that spot  which i point  paradise adams abode those loftie shades his bowre thy way thou canst not miss me mine requires thus said  turnd  satan bowing low as  superior spirits  wont  heaven where honour due  reverence none neglects took leave  toward  coast  earth beneath down  th’ ecliptic sped  hop’d success throws his steep flight  many  aerie wheele nor staid till  niphates top  lights the end of the third book paradise lost book iv o for  warning voice which  who saw th’ apocalyps heard cry  heaven aloud then when  dragon put  second rout came furious down   reveng’d  men wo   inhabitants  earth  now while time was our first parents had bin warnd the coming  thir secret foe  scap’d haply so scap’d his mortal snare  now satan now first inflam’d  rage came down the tempter ere th’ accuser  mankind to wreck  innocent frail man his loss of  first battel  his flight  hell yet not rejoycing  his speed though bold far off  fearless nor  cause  boast begins his dire attempt which nigh  birth now rowling boiles  his tumultuous brest and like  devillish engine back recoiles upon himself horror  doubt distract his troubl’d thoughts    bottom stirr the hell within him  within him hell he brings  round about him nor  hell one step no more then  himself can fly by change  place now conscience wakes despair that slumberd wakes  bitter memorie of what  was what is  what must  worse  worse deeds worse sufferings must ensue sometimes towards eden which now  his view lay pleasant his grievd look  fixes sad sometimes towards heav’n   fullblazing sun which now sat high  his meridian towre then much revolving thus  sighs began o thou   surpassing glory crownd look’st  thy sole dominion like  god of this new world  whose sight all  starrs hide thir diminisht heads  thee i call but  no friendly voice  add thy name o sun  tell thee how i hate thy beams that bring  my remembrance  what state i fell how glorious once above thy spheare till pride  worse ambition threw me down warring  heav’n against heav’ns matchless king ah wherefore  deservd no such return from me whom  created what i  in  bright eminence   his good upbraided none nor  his service hard what could  less then  afford him praise the easiest recompence  pay him thanks how due yet all his good prov’d ill  me and wrought but malice lifted up so high i sdeind subjection  thought one step higher would set me highest    moment quit the debt immense  endless gratitude so burthensome still paying still  ow forgetful what  him i still receivd and understood not   grateful mind by owing owes not but still pays  once indebted  dischargd what burden then o had his powerful destiny ordaind me some inferiour angel i had stood then happie no unbounded hope had rais’d ambition yet why not som other power as great might have aspir’d  me though mean drawn  his part but other powers  great fell not but stand unshak’n  within or  without  all temptations arm’d hadst thou  same free will  power  stand thou hadst whom hast thou then or what  accuse but heav’ns free love dealt equally  all be then his love accurst since love or hate to me alike  deals eternal woe nay curs’d  thou since against his thy  chose freely what  now so justly rues me miserable which way shall i flie infinite wrauth  infinite despaire which way i flie  hell my self am hell and   lowest deep  lower deep still threatning  devour me opens wide to which  hell i suffer seems  heav’n o then  last relent  there no place left  repentance none  pardon left none left but  submission   word disdain forbids me  my dread  shame among  spirits beneath whom i seduc’d with other promises  other vaunts then  submit boasting i could subdue th’ omnipotent ay me they little know how dearly i abide  boast so vaine under what torments inwardly i groane while they adore me   throne  hell with diadem  scepter high advanc’d the lower still i fall onely supream in miserie such joy ambition findes but say i could repent  could obtaine by act  grace my former state how soon would highth recal high thoughts how soon unsay what feign’d submission swore ease would recant vows made  pain  violent  void for never can true reconcilement grow where wounds  deadly hate have peirc’d so deep which would but lead me   worse relapse and heavier fall so should i purchase deare short intermission bought  double smart this knows my punisher therefore  farr from granting hee  i  begging peace all hope excluded thus behold  stead of us outcast exil’d his new delight mankind created   him this world so farwel hope   hope farwel fear farwel remorse all good  me  lost evil  thou my good  thee  least divided empire  heav’ns king i hold by thee  more then half perhaps  reigne as man ere long  this new world shall know thus while  spake each passion dimm’d his face us this ample world be infinitly good   his good as liberal  free  infinite that rais’d us   dust  plac’t us here in all this happiness who  his hand have nothing merited nor can performe aught whom thus eve repli’d o thou  whom and  whom i  formd flesh  thy flesh and without whom am  no end my guide and head what thou hast said  just  right for wee  him indeed all praises owe and daily thanks i chiefly who enjoy so farr  happier lot enjoying thee preeminent  so much odds while thou like consort  thy self canst no where find that day i oft remember when  sleep i first awak’t  found my self repos’d under  shade  flours much wondring where and what i was whence thither brought  how not distant far  thence  murmuring sound of waters issu’d   cave  spread into  liquid plain then stood unmov’d pure  th’ expanse  heav’n i thither went with unexperienc’t thought  laid me downe on  green bank  look into  cleer smooth lake   me seemd another skie as i bent down  look just opposite a shape within  watry gleam appeerd bending  look  me i started back it started back but pleasd i soon returnd pleas’d  returnd  soon  answering looks of sympathie  love there i had fixt mine eyes till now  pin’d  vain desire had not  voice thus warnd me what thou seest what there thou seest fair creature  thy self with thee  came  goes but follow me and i  bring thee where no shadow staies thy coming  thy soft imbraces hee whose image thou art him thou shall enjoy inseparablie thine  him shalt beare multitudes like thy self  thence  call’d mother  human race what could i doe but follow strait invisibly thus led till i espi’d thee fair indeed  tall under  platan yet methought less faire less winning soft less amiablie milde then  smooth watry image back i turnd thou following cryd’st aloud return fair eve whom fli’st thou whom thou fli’st  him thou art his flesh his bone  give thee being i lent out  my side  thee neerest my heart substantial life  have thee  my side henceforth  individual solace dear part  my soul i seek thee  thee claim my other half   thy gentle hand seisd mine i yeilded    time see how beauty  excelld  manly grace and wisdom which alone  truly fair so spake our general mother   eyes of conjugal attraction unreprov’d and meek surrender half imbracing leand on our first father half her swelling breast naked met his under  flowing gold of her loose tresses hid   delight both  her beauty  submissive charms smil’d  superior love  jupiter on juno smiles when  impregns  clouds that shed may flowers  press’d her matron lip with kisses pure aside  devil turnd for envie yet  jealous leer maligne ey’d them askance   himself thus plaind sight hateful sight tormenting thus these two imparadis’t  one anothers arms the happier eden shall enjoy thir fill of bliss  bliss while i  hell am thrust where neither joy nor love but fierce desire among our other torments not  least still unfulfill’d  pain  longing pines yet let me not forget what i have gain’d from thir own mouths all  not theirs  seems one fatal tree there stands  knowledge call’d forbidden them  taste knowledge forbidd’n suspicious reasonless why should thir lord envie them that can   sin  know can   death  do they onely stand by ignorance   thir happie state the proof  thir obedience  thir faith o fair foundation laid whereon  build thir ruine hence i  excite thir minds with more desire  know   reject envious commands invented  designe to keep them low whom knowledge might exalt equal  gods aspiring   such they taste  die what likelier can ensue but first  narrow search i must walk round this garden  no corner leave unspi’d a chance but chance may lead where i may meet some wandring spirit  heav’n  fountain side or  thick shade retir’d  him  draw what further would  learnt live while ye may yet happie pair enjoy till i return short pleasures  long woes   succeed so saying his proud step  scornful turn’d but  sly circumspection  began through wood through waste o’re hil o’re dale his roam mean while  utmost longitude where heav’n with earth  ocean meets  setting sun slowly descended   right aspect against  eastern gate  paradise leveld his eevning rayes    rock of alablaster pil’d up   clouds conspicuous farr winding  one ascent accessible  earth one entrance high the rest  craggie cliff  overhung still   rose impossible  climbe betwixt these rockie pillars gabriel sat chief  th’ angelic guards awaiting night about him exercis’d heroic games th’ unarmed youth  heav’n but nigh  hand celestial armourie shields helmes  speares hung high  diamond flaming   gold thither came uriel gliding through  eeven on  sun beam swift   shooting starr in autumn thwarts  night when vapors fir’d impress  air  shews  mariner from what point  his compass  beware impetuous winds  thus began  haste gabriel  thee thy cours  lot hath giv’n charge  strict watch   this happie place no evil thing approach or enter in this day  highth  noon came  my spheare a spirit zealous   seem’d  know more  th’ almighties works  chiefly man gods latest image i describ’d his way bent all  speed  markt his aerie gate but   mount  lies  eden north where  first lighted soon discernd his looks alien  heav’n  passions foul obscur’d mine eye pursu’d him still but under shade lost sight  him one   banisht crew i fear hath ventur’d   deep  raise new troubles him thy care must   find to whom  winged warriour thus returnd uriel no wonder if thy perfet sight amid  suns bright circle where thou sitst see farr  wide   this gate none pass the vigilance here plac’t but such  come well known  heav’n  since meridian hour no creature thence if spirit  other sort so minded have oreleapt these earthie bounds on purpose hard thou knowst   exclude spiritual substance  corporeal barr but if within  circuit  these walks in whatsoever shape  lurk  whom thou telst  morrow dawning i shall know so promis’d hee  uriel  his charge returnd   bright beam whose point now raisd bore him slope downward   sun now fall’n beneath th’ azores whither  prime orb incredible how swift had thither rowl’d diurnal or this less volubil earth by shorter flight  th’ east had left him there arraying  reflected purple  gold the clouds   his western throne attend now came still eevning on  twilight gray had  her sober liverie all things clad silence accompanied  beast  bird they  thir grassie couch these  thir nests were slunk all but  wakeful nightingale she all night long her amorous descant sung silence  pleas’d now glow’d  firmament with living saphirs hesperus  led the starrie host rode brightest till  moon rising  clouded majestie  length apparent queen unvaild her peerless light and o’re  dark her silver mantle threw when adam thus  eve fair consort th’ hour of night  all things now retir’d  rest mind us  like repose since god hath set labour  rest  day  night  men successive   timely dew  sleep now falling  soft slumbrous weight inclines our eyelids other creatures all day long rove idle unimploid  less need rest man hath his daily work  body or mind appointed which declares his dignitie and  regard  heav’n  all his waies while other animals unactive range and  thir doings god takes no account tomorrow ere fresh morning streak  east with first approach  light we must  ris’n and  our pleasant labour  reform yon flourie arbors yonder allies green our walks  noon  branches overgrown that mock our scant manuring  require more hands then ours  lop thir wanton growth those blossoms also  those dropping gumms that lie bestrowne unsightly  unsmooth ask riddance if we mean  tread  ease mean while  nature wills night bids us rest to whom thus eve  perfet beauty adornd my author  disposer what thou bidst unargu’d i obey so god ordains god  thy law thou mine  know no more is womans happiest knowledge  her praise with thee conversing i forget all time all seasons  thir change all please alike sweet   breath  morn her rising sweet with charm  earliest birds pleasant  sun when first  this delightful land  spreads his orient beams  herb tree fruit  flour glistring  dew fragrant  fertil earth after soft showers  sweet  coming  of grateful eevning milde then silent night with this her solemn bird  this fair moon and these  gemms  heav’n her starrie train but neither breath  morn when she ascends with charm  earliest birds nor rising sun on this delightful land nor herb fruit floure glistring  dew nor fragrance after showers nor grateful evening mild nor silent night with this her solemn bird nor walk  moon or glittering starrlight without thee  sweet but wherfore all night long shine these  whom this glorious sight when sleep hath shut all eyes to whom our general ancestor repli’d daughter  god  man accomplisht eve those have thir course  finish round  earth by morrow eevning   land  land in order though  nations yet unborn ministring light prepar’d they set  rise least total darkness should  night regaine her old possession  extinguish life in nature  all things which these soft fires not only enlighten but  kindly heate of various influence foment  warme temper or nourish or  part shed down thir stellar vertue  all kinds  grow on earth made hereby apter  receive perfection   suns more potent ray these then though unbeheld  deep  night shine not  vain nor think though men  none that heav’n would want spectators god want praise millions  spiritual creatures walk  earth unseen both when we wake  when we sleep all these  ceasless praise his works behold both day  night how often   steep of echoing hill or thicket have we heard celestial voices   midnight air sole or responsive each  others note singing thir great creator oft  bands while they keep watch or nightly rounding walk with heav’nly touch  instrumental sounds in full harmonic number joind thir songs divide  night  lift our thoughts  heaven thus talking hand  hand alone they pass’d on  thir blissful bower    place chos’n   sovran planter when  fram’d all things  mans delightful use  roofe of thickest covert  inwoven shade laurel  mirtle  what higher grew of firm  fragrant leaf  either side acanthus  each odorous bushie shrub fenc’d up  verdant wall each beauteous flour iris all hues roses  gessamin rear’d high thir flourisht heads between  wrought mosaic underfoot  violet crocus  hyacinth  rich inlay broiderd  ground more colour’d then  stone of costliest emblem other creature here beast bird insect or worm durst enter none such  thir awe  man in shadier bower more sacred  sequesterd though but feignd pan or silvanus never slept nor nymph nor faunus haunted here  close recess with flowers garlands  sweetsmelling herbs espoused eve deckt first her nuptial bed and heav’nly quires  hymenaean sung what day  genial angel  our sire brought her  naked beauty more adorn’d more lovely then pandora whom  gods endowd  all thir gifts  o too like in sad event when   unwiser son of japhet brought  hermes she ensnar’d mankind  her faire looks   aveng’d on him who had stole joves authentic fire thus  thir shadie lodge arriv’d both stood both turnd  under op’n skie ador’d the god  made both skie air earth  heav’n which they beheld  moons resplendent globe and starrie pole thou also mad’st  night maker omnipotent  thou  day which we  our appointed work imployd have finisht happie  our mutual help and mutual love  crown  all our bliss ordain’d  thee  this delicious place for us too large where thy abundance wants partakers  uncropt falls   ground but thou hast promis’d  us two  race to fill  earth who shall  us extoll thy goodness infinite both when we wake and when we seek  now thy gift  sleep this said unanimous  other rites observing none but adoration pure which god likes best into thir inmost bower handed they went  eas’d  putting off these troublesom disguises which wee wear strait side  side  laid nor turnd i weene adam  his fair spouse nor eve  rites mysterious  connubial love refus’d whatever hypocrites austerely talk of puritie  place  innocence defaming  impure what god declares pure  commands  som leaves free  all our maker bids increase who bids abstain but our destroyer foe  god  man haile wedded love mysterious law true source of human ofspring sole proprietie in paradise  all things common else by thee adulterous lust  driv’n  men among  bestial herds  raunge  thee founded  reason loyal just  pure relations dear  all  charities of father son  brother first  known farr  it  i should write thee sin or blame or think thee unbefitting holiest place perpetual fountain  domestic sweets whose bed  undefil’d  chast pronounc’t present or past  saints  patriarchs us’d here love his golden shafts imploies here lights his constant lamp  waves his purple wings reigns here  revels not   bought smile of harlots loveless joyless unindeard casual fruition nor  court amours mixt dance or wanton mask or midnight bal or serenate which  starv’d lover sings to his proud fair best quitted  disdain these lulld  nightingales imbraceing slept and  thir naked limbs  flourie roof showrd roses which  morn repair’d sleep on blest pair  o yet happiest if ye seek no happier state  know  know no more now had night measur’d  her shaddowie cone half way up hill this vast sublunar vault and  thir ivorie port  cherubim forth issuing  th’ accustomd hour stood armd to thir night watches  warlike parade when gabriel  his next  power thus spake uzziel half these draw off  coast  south with strictest watch these other wheel  north our circuit meets full west as flame they part half wheeling   shield half two fair creatures lodge now laid perhaps asleep secure  harme this eevning   sun’s decline arriv’d who tells  som infernal spirit seen hitherward bent who could have thought escap’d the barrs  hell  errand bad no doubt such where ye find seise fast  hither bring so saying   led his radiant files daz’ling  moon these   bower direct in search  whom they sought him there they found squat like  toad close   eare  eve assaying  his devilish art  reach the organs  her fancie   them forge illusions   list phantasms  dreams or if inspiring venom  might taint th’ animal spirits   pure blood arise like these  sleep know ye not then said satan filld  scorn know ye not me ye knew me once no mate for you there sitting where ye durst not soare not  know mee argues your selves unknown the lowest  your throng or if ye know why ask ye  superfluous begin your message like  end  much  vain to whom thus zephon answering scorn  scorn think not revolted spirit thy shape  same or undiminisht brightness awful goodness is  saw vertue  her shape how lovly saw  pin’d his loss but chiefly  find here observd his lustre visibly impar’d yet seemd undaunted if i must contend said he best   best  sender not like  proud steed reind went hautie on chaumping his iron curb  strive or flie he held  vain awe  above had quelld his heart not else dismai’d now drew they nigh the western point where those halfrounding guards just met  closing stood  squadron joind awaiting next command to whom thir chief gabriel   front thus calld aloud o friends i hear  tread  nimble feet hasting this way  now  glimps firm   his look defiance lours he scarce had ended when those two approachd and brief related whom they brought wher found how busied  what form  posture coucht to whom  stern regard thus gabriel spake why hast thou satan broke  bounds prescrib’d to thy transgressions  disturbd  charge of others who approve not  transgress by thy example but have power  right to question thy bold entrance  this place imploi’d  seems  violate sleep  those whose dwelling god hath planted here  bliss to whom thus satan  contemptuous brow gabriel thou hadst  heav’n th’ esteem  wise and such i held thee but this question askt puts me  doubt lives ther who loves his pain who would not finding way break loose  hell though thither doomd thou wouldst thy self no doubt and boldly venture  whatever place farthest  pain where thou mightst hope  change torment  ease  soonest recompence dole  delight which  this place i sought to thee no reason who knowst only good but evil hast not tri’d  wilt object his  who bound us let him surer barr his iron gates if  intends our stay in  dark durance thus much what  askt the rest  true they found me where they say but  implies not violence or harme thus hee  scorn the warlike angel mov’d disdainfully half smiling thus repli’d o loss  one  heav’n  judge  wise since satan fell whom follie overthrew and now returns him  his prison scap’t gravely  doubt whether  hold them wise or not who ask what boldness brought him hither unlicenc’t  his bounds  hell prescrib’d so wise  judges   fly  pain however   scape his punishment so judge thou still presumptuous till  wrauth which thou incurr’st  flying meet thy flight seavenfold  scourge  wisdom back  hell which taught thee yet no better  no pain can equal anger infinite provok’t but wherefore thou alone wherefore  thee came not all hell broke loose  pain  them less pain less   fled or thou then they less hardie  endure courageous chief the first  flight  pain had’st thou alleg’d to thy deserted host this cause  flight thou surely hadst not come sole fugitive to which  fiend thus answerd frowning stern not  i less endure or shrink  pain insulting angel well thou knowst i stood thy fiercest when  battel  thy aide the blasting volied thunder made all speed and seconded thy else not dreaded spear but still thy words  random  before argue thy inexperience what behooves from hard assaies  ill successes past a faithful leader not  hazard all through wayes  danger  himself untri’d i therefore i alone first undertook to wing  desolate abyss  spie this new created world whereof  hell fame  not silent here  hope  find better abode  my afflicted powers to settle here  earth or  mid aire though  possession put  try once more what thou  thy gay legions dare against whose easier business   serve thir lord high up  heav’n  songs  hymne his throne and practis’d distances  cringe not fight to whom  warriour angel soon repli’d to say  strait unsay pretending first wise  flie pain professing next  spie argues no leader but  lyar trac’t satan  couldst thou faithful add o name o sacred name  faithfulness profan’d faithful  whom  thy rebellious crew armie  fiends fit body  fit head was this your discipline  faith ingag’d your military obedience  dissolve allegeance  th’ acknowledg’d power supream and thou sly hypocrite who now wouldst seem patron  liberty who more then thou once fawn’d  cring’d  servilly ador’d heav’ns awful monarch wherefore but  hope to dispossess him  thy self  reigne but mark what i arreede thee now avant flie thither whence thou fledst if  this houre within these hallowd limits thou appeer back  th’ infernal pit i drag thee chaind and seale thee so  henceforth not  scorne the facil gates  hell too slightly barrd so threatn’d hee but satan  no threats gave heed but waxing more  rage repli’d then when i am thy captive talk  chaines proud limitarie cherube but ere then farr heavier load thy self expect  feel from my prevailing arme though heavens king ride  thy wings  thou  thy compeers us’d   yoak draw’st his triumphant wheels in progress through  rode  heav’n starpav’d while thus  spake th’ angelic squadron bright turnd fierie red sharpning  mooned hornes thir phalanx  began  hemm him round with ported spears  thick  when  field of ceres ripe  harvest waving bends her bearded grove  ears which way  wind swayes them  careful reacht  skie   his crest sat horror plum’d nor wanted  his graspe what seemd both spear  shield now dreadful deeds might have ensu’d nor onely paradise in this commotion but  starrie cope of heav’n perhaps or all  elements at least had gon  rack disturbd  torne with violence  this conflict had not soon th’ eternal  prevent such horrid fray hung forth  heav’n his golden scales yet seen betwixt astrea   scorpion signe wherein all things created first  weighd the pendulous round earth  ballanc’t aire in counterpoise now ponders all events battels  realms  these  put two weights the sequel each  parting   fight the latter quick up flew  kickt  beam which gabriel spying thus bespake  fiend satan i know thy strength  thou knowst mine neither our own but giv’n what follie then to boast what arms can doe since thine no more then heav’n permits nor mine though doubld now to trample thee  mire  proof look up and read thy lot  yon celestial sign where thou art weigh’d  shown how light how weak if thou resist the fiend lookt up  knew his mounted scale aloft nor more but fled murmuring   him fled  shades  night the end of the fourth book paradise lost book v now morn her rosie steps  th’ eastern clime advancing sow’d  earth  orient pearle when adam wak’t so customd  his sleep was aerie light  pure digestion bred and temperat vapors bland which th’ only sound of leaves  fuming rills aurora’s fan lightly dispers’d   shrill matin song of birds  every bough so much  more his wonder   find unwak’nd eve with tresses discompos’d  glowing cheek as through unquiet rest   his side leaning halfrais’d  looks  cordial love hung over her enamour’d  beheld beautie which whether waking or asleep shot forth peculiar graces then  voice milde  when zephyrus  flora breathes her hand soft touching whisperd thus awake my fairest my espous’d my latest found heav’ns last best gift my ever new delight awake  morning shines   fresh field calls us we lose  prime  mark how spring our tended whom imbracing thus she spake o sole  whom my thoughts find all repose my glorie my perfection glad i see thy face  morn return’d  i this night such night till this i never pass’d have dream’d if dream’d not  i oft am wont  thee works  day pass’t or morrows next designe but  offence  trouble which my mind knew never till this irksom night methought close  mine ear one call’d me forth  walk with gentle voice i thought  thine  said why sleepst thou eve now   pleasant time the cool  silent save where silence yields to  nightwarbling bird  now awake tunes sweetest his lovelabor’d song now reignes full orb’d  moon   more pleasing light shadowie sets off  face  things  vain if none regard heav’n wakes  all his eyes whom  behold but thee natures desire in whose sight all things joy  ravishment attracted  thy beauty still  gaze i rose   thy call but found thee not to find thee i directed then my walk and on methought alone i pass’d through ways that brought me   sudden   tree of interdicted knowledge fair  seem’d much fairer  my fancie then  day and  i wondring lookt beside  stood one shap’d  wing’d like one  those  heav’n by us oft seen his dewie locks distill’d ambrosia none shall  me withhold longer thy offerd good why else set here this said  paus’d not but  ventrous arme he pluckt  tasted mee damp horror chil’d at such bold words voucht   deed so bold but  thus overjoy’d o fruit divine sweet  thy self but much more sweet thus cropt forbidd’n here  seems  onely fit for gods yet able  make gods  men and why not gods  men since good  more communicated more abundant growes the author not impair’d but honourd more here happie creature fair angelic eve partake thou also happie though thou art happier thou mayst be worthier canst not be taste this   henceforth among  gods thy self  goddess not  earth confind but somtimes   air  wee somtimes ascend  heav’n  merit thine  see what life  gods live there  such live thou so saying  drew nigh   me held even  my mouth   same fruit held part which  had pluckt  pleasant savourie smell so quick’nd appetite  i methought could not but taste forthwith up   clouds with him i flew  underneath beheld the earth outstretcht immense  prospect wide and various wondring  my flight  change to this high exaltation suddenly my guide  gon  i me thought sunk down and fell asleep but o how glad i wak’d to find this but  dream thus eve her night related  thus adam answerd sad best image  my self  dearer half the trouble  thy thoughts this night  sleep affects me equally nor can i like this uncouth dream  evil sprung i fear yet evil whence  thee can harbour none created pure but know    soule are many lesser faculties  serve reason  chief among these fansie next her office holds  all external things which  five watchful senses represent she forms imaginations aerie shapes which reason joyning or disjoyning frames all what we affirm or what deny  call our knowledge or opinion then retires into her private cell when nature rests oft  her absence mimic fansie wakes to imitate her but misjoyning shapes wilde work produces oft  most  dreams ill matching words  deeds long past or late som such resemblances methinks i find of our last eevnings talk  this thy dream but  addition strange yet  not sad evil into  mind  god or man may come  go so unapprov’d  leave no spot or blame behind which gives me hope that what  sleep thou didst abhorr  dream waking thou never wilt consent  do be not disheart’nd then nor cloud those looks that wont   more chearful  serene then when fair morning first withstood but  deceit  lies this let him know least wilfully transgressing  pretend surprisal unadmonisht unforewarnd so spake th’ eternal father  fulfilld all justice nor delaid  winged saint after starr interpos’d however small  sees not unconform  other shining globes earth   gard’n  god  cedars crownd above all hills as when  night  glass of galileo less assur’d observes imagind lands thy kingdom let mee serve in heav’n god ever blessed  his divine behests obey worthiest   obey’d yet chains  hell not realms expect mean while from mee returnd  erst thou saidst  flight this greeting intercept ten paces huge he back recoild  tenth  bended knee his massie spear upstaid  if  earth winds under ground or waters forcing way sidelong had push’t  mountain  his seat half sunk  all his fathers might ascend my chariot guide  rapid wheeles that shake heav’ns basis bring forth all my warr my bow  thunder my almightie arms gird on  sword upon thy puissant thigh pursue these sons  darkness drive them out from all heav’ns bounds into  utter deep there let them learn  likes them  despise god  messiah his anointed king he said   his son  rayes direct shon full  all his father full exprest ineffably into his face receiv’d and thus  filial godhead answering spake o father o supream  heav’nly thrones first highest holiest best thou alwayes seekst to glorifie thy son i alwayes thee as  most just this i my glorie account my exaltation  my whole delight that thou  me well pleas’d declarst thy  fulfill’d which  fulfil  all my bliss scepter  power thy giving i assume and gladlier shall resign when   end thou shalt  all  all  i  thee for ever   mee all whom thou lov’st but whom thou hat’st i hate  can put  thy terrors  i put thy mildness on image  thee  all things  shall soon transgress the end of the sixth book paradise lost book vii descend  heav’n urania   name if rightly thou art call’d whose voice divine following above th’ olympian hill i soare above  flight tempring  like safetie guided down return me  my native element least  this flying steed unrein’d as once bellerophon though   lower clime dismounted  th’ aleian field i fall erroneous there  wander sire   his count’nance seemd entring  studious thoughts abstruse which eve perceaving where she sat retir’d  sight with lowliness majestic  her seat and grace  won who saw  wish her stay rose  went forth among her fruits  flours to visit how they prosper’d bud  bloom her nurserie they  her coming sprung and toucht  her fair tendance gladlier grew yet went she not  not  such discourse delighted or not capable her eare of what  high such pleasure she reserv’d adam relating she sole auditress her husband  relater she preferr’d before  angel   him  ask chose rather hee she knew would intermix repli’d to ask or search i blame thee not  heav’n is   book  god before thee set wherein  read his wondrous works  learne his seasons hours or days or months or yeares this  attain whether heav’n move or earth imports not if thou reck’n right  rest from man or angel  great architect did wisely  conceal  not divulge his secrets   scann’d  them who ought rather admire or if they list  try conjecture  his fabric   heav’ns hath left  thir disputes perhaps  move his laughter  thir quaint opinions wide hereafter when they come  model heav’n and calculate  starrs how they  weild the mightie frame how excellence  earth though  comparison  heav’n so small nor glistering may  solid good containe more plenty then  sun  barren shines whose vertue   self workes no effect but   fruitful earth there first so spacious  his line stretcht out so farr that man may know  dwells not  his own an edifice too large  him  fill lodg’d   small partition   rest ordain’d  uses  his lord best known the swiftness  those circles attribute though numberless  his omnipotence that  corporeal substances could adde speed almost spiritual mee thou thinkst not slow who since  morning hour set out  heav’n where god by living soule desert  desolate onely  shine yet scarce  contribute each orb  glimps  light conveyd so farr down  this habitable which returnes light back  them  obvious  dispute but whether thus these things or whether not whether  sun predominant  heav’n rise   earth or earth rise   sun hee   east his flaming rode begin or shee  west her silent course advance with inoffensive pace  spinning
