dream not  other worlds what creatures there live  what state condition or degree contented  thus farr hath been reveal’d not  earth onely but  highest heav’n to whom thus adam cleerd  doubt repli’d how fully hast thou satisfi’d mee pure intelligence  heav’n angel serene and freed  intricacies taught  live the easiest way nor  perplexing thoughts to interrupt  sweet  life  which god hath bid dwell farr off all anxious cares and not molest us unless we our selves seek them  wandring thoughts  notions vaine but apt  mind or fancie   roave uncheckt   her roaving  no end till warn’d or  experience taught she learne that not  know  large  things remote from use obscure  suttle but  know that which before us lies  daily life is  prime wisdom what  more  fume or emptiness or fond impertinence and renders us  things  most concerne unpractis’d unprepar’d  still  seek therefore  this high pitch let us descend a lower flight  speak  things  hand useful whence haply mention may arise of somthing not unseasonable  ask by sufferance  thy wonted favour deign’d thee i have heard relating what  don ere my remembrance now hear mee relate my storie which perhaps thou hast not heard and day  yet not spent till then thou seest how suttly  detaine thee i devise inviting thee  hear while i relate fond   not  hope  thy reply for while i sit  thee i seem  heav’n and sweeter thy discourse   my eare then fruits  palmtree pleasantest  thirst and hunger both  labour   houre of sweet repast they satiate  soon fill though pleasant but thy words  grace divine imbu’d bring  thir sweetness no satietie to whom thus raphael answer’d heav’nly meek nor  thy lips ungraceful sire  men nor tongue ineloquent  god  thee abundantly his gifts hath also pour’d inward  outward both his image faire speaking or mute all comliness  grace attends thee  each word each motion formes nor less think wee  heav’n  thee  earth then  our fellow servant  inquire gladly into  wayes  god  man for god we see hath honour’d thee  set on man his equal love say therefore on for i  day  absent  befell bound   voyage uncouth  obscure farr  excursion toward  gates  hell squar’d  full legion such command we had to see  none thence issu’d forth  spie or enemie while god   his work least hee incenst  such eruption bold destruction  creation might have mixt not  they durst without his leave attempt but us  sends upon his high behests for state  sovran king   enure our prompt obedience fast we found fast shut the dismal gates  barricado’d strong but long ere our approaching heard within noise other then  sound  dance or song torment  lowd lament  furious rage glad we return’d up   coasts  light ere sabbath eev’ning so we had  charge but thy relation now  i attend pleas’d  thy words no less then thou  mine so spake  godlike power  thus our sire for man  tell how human life began is hard  who himself beginning knew desire  thee still longer  converse induc’d me as new wak’t  soundest sleep soft   flourie herb i found me laid in balmie sweat which  his beames  sun soon dri’d    reaking moisture fed strait toward heav’n my wondring eyes i turnd and gaz’d  while  ample skie till rais’d by quick instinctive motion up i sprung as thitherward endevoring  upright stood  my feet about me round i saw hill dale  shadie woods  sunnie plaines and liquid lapse  murmuring streams  these creatures  livd  movd  walk’d or flew birds   branches warbling all things smil’d with fragrance   joy my heart oreflow’d my self i then perus’d  limb  limb survey’d  sometimes went  sometimes ran with supple joints  lively vigour led but who i was or where or  what cause knew not  speak i tri’d  forthwith spake my tongue obey’d  readily could name what e’re i saw thou sun said i faire light and thou enlight’nd earth so fresh  gay ye hills  dales ye rivers woods  plaines and ye  live  move fair creatures tell tell if ye saw how came i thus how here not  my self  some great maker then in goodness   power praeeminent tell me how may i know him how adore from whom i have  thus i move  live and feel  i am happier then i know while thus i call’d  stray’d i knew not whither from where i first drew aire  first beheld this happie light when answer none return’d on  green shadie bank profuse  flours pensive i sate me down there gentle sleep first found me   soft oppression seis’d my droused sense untroubl’d though i thought i then  passing  my former state insensible  forthwith  dissolve when suddenly stood  my head  dream whose inward apparition gently mov’d my fancy  believe i yet had being and livd one came methought  shape divine and said thy mansion wants thee adam rise first man  men innumerable ordain’d first father call’d  thee i come thy guide to  garden  bliss thy seat prepar’d so saying   hand  took me rais’d and over fields  waters   aire smooth sliding without step last led me up a woodie mountain whose high top  plaine a circuit wide enclos’d  goodliest trees planted  walks  bowers  what i saw of earth before scarse pleasant seemd each tree load’n  fairest fruit  hung   eye tempting stirr’d  me sudden appetite to pluck  eate whereat i wak’d  found before mine eyes all real   dream had lively shadowd here had new begun my wandring had not hee who  my guide up hither  among  trees appeer’d presence divine rejoycing but  aw in adoration  his feet i fell submiss  rear’d me  whom thou soughtst i am said mildely author  all this thou seest above or round about thee or beneath this paradise i give thee count  thine to till  keep    fruit  eate of every tree    garden growes eate freely  glad heart fear here no dearth but   tree whose operation brings knowledg  good  ill which i have set the pledge  thy obedience  thy faith amid  garden   tree  life remember what i warne thee shun  taste and shun  bitter consequence  know the day thou eat’st thereof my sole command transgrest inevitably thou shalt dye from  day mortal  this happie state shalt loose expell’d  hence into  world of woe  sorrow sternly  pronounc’d the rigid interdiction which resounds yet dreadful  mine eare though  my choice not  incur but soon his cleer aspect return’d  gratious purpose thus renew’d not onely these fair bounds but all  earth to thee   thy race i give  lords possess it  all things  therein live or live  sea or aire beast fish  fowle in signe whereof each bird  beast behold after thir kindes i bring them  receave from thee thir names  pay thee fealtie with low subjection understand  same of fish within thir watry residence not hither summond since they cannot change thir element  draw  thinner aire as thus  spake each bird  beast behold approaching two  two these cowring low with blandishment each bird stoop’d  his wing i nam’d them  they pass’d  understood thir nature  such knowledg god endu’d my sudden apprehension but  these i found not what me thought i wanted still and   heav’nly vision thus presum’d o  what name  thou above all these above mankinde or aught then mankinde higher surpassest farr my naming how may i adore thee author  this universe and all this good  man  whose well being so amply   hands so liberal thou hast provided all things but  mee i see not who partakes in solitude what happiness who can enjoy alone or all enjoying what contentment find thus i presumptuous   vision bright as   smile more bright’nd thus repli’d what call’st thou solitude  not  earth with various living creatures   aire replenisht  all these  thy command to come  play before thee know’st thou not thir language  thir wayes they also know and reason not contemptibly  these find pastime  beare rule thy realm  large so spake  universal lord  seem’d so ordering i  leave  speech implor’d and humble deprecation thus repli’d let not my words offend thee heav’nly power my maker  propitious while i speak hast thou not made me here thy substitute and these inferiour farr beneath me set among unequals what societie can sort what harmonie or true delight which must  mutual  proportion due giv’n  receiv’d but  disparitie the one intense  other still remiss cannot well suite  either but soon prove tedious alike of fellowship i speak such  i seek fit  participate all rational delight wherein  brute cannot  human consort they rejoyce each  thir kinde lion  lioness so fitly them  pairs thou hast combin’d much less can bird  beast or fish  fowle so well converse nor   ox  ape wors then can man  beast  least  all whereto th’ almighty answer’d not displeas’d a nice  suttle happiness i see thou  thy self proposest   choice of thy associates adam  wilt taste no pleasure though  pleasure solitarie what thinkst thou then  mee  this my state seem i  thee sufficiently possest of happiness or not who am alone from all eternitie  none i know second  mee or like equal much less how have i then  whom  hold converse save   creatures which i made  those to me inferiour infinite descents beneath what other creatures   thee he ceas’d i lowly answer’d to attaine the highth  depth  thy eternal wayes all human thoughts come short supream  things thou  thy self art perfet   thee is no deficience found not so  man but  degree  cause  his desire by conversation  his like  help or solace his defects no need  thou shouldst propagat already infinite and through all numbers absolute though one but man  number   manifest his single imperfection  beget like  his like his image multipli’d in unitie defective which requires collateral love  deerest amitie thou  thy secresie although alone best  thy self accompanied seek’st not social communication yet so pleas’d canst raise thy creature  what highth thou wilt of union or communion deifi’d i  conversing cannot these erect from prone nor  thir wayes complacence find thus i embold’nd spake  freedom us’d permissive  acceptance found which gain’d this answer   gratious voice divine thus farr  try thee adam i  pleas’d and finde thee knowing not  beasts alone which thou hast rightly nam’d but  thy self expressing well  spirit within thee free my image not imparted   brute whose fellowship therefore unmeet  thee good reason  thou freely shouldst dislike and  so minded still i ere thou spak’st knew  not good  man   alone and no such companie  then thou saw’st intended thee  trial onely brought to see how thou could’st judge  fit  meet what next i bring shall please thee  assur’d thy likeness thy fit help thy other self thy wish exactly  thy hearts desire hee ended or i heard no more  now my earthly  his heav’nly overpowerd which  had long stood under streind   highth in  celestial colloquie sublime as   object  excels  sense dazl’d  spent sunk down  sought repair of sleep which instantly fell  me call’d by nature   aide  clos’d mine eyes mine eyes  clos’d but op’n left  cell of fancie my internal sight  which abstract    transe methought i saw though sleeping where i lay  saw  shape still glorious before whom awake i stood who stooping op’nd my left side  took from thence  rib  cordial spirits warme and lifeblood streaming fresh wide   wound but suddenly  flesh fill’d up  heal’d the rib  formd  fashond  his hands under his forming hands  creature grew manlike but different sex so lovly faire that what seemd fair  all  world seemd now mean or  her summd up  her containd and  her looks which   time infus’d sweetness into my heart unfelt before and into all things  her aire inspir’d the spirit  love  amorous delight she disappeerd  left me dark i wak’d to find her or  ever  deplore her loss  other pleasures all abjure when out  hope behold her not farr off such  i saw her  my dream adornd with what all earth or heaven could bestow to make her amiable on she came led  her heav’nly maker though unseen and guided  his voice nor uninformd of nuptial sanctitie  marriage rites grace   all her steps heav’n  her eye in every gesture dignitie  love i overjoyd could not forbear aloud this turn hath made amends thou hast fulfill’d thy words creator bounteous  benigne giver  all things faire but fairest this of all thy gifts nor enviest i now see bone  my bone flesh  my flesh my self before me woman  her name  man extracted  this cause  shall forgoe father  mother   his wife adhere and they shall  one flesh one heart one soule she heard me thus  though divinely brought yet innocence  virgin modestie her vertue   conscience  her worth that would  woo’d  not unsought  won not obvious not obtrusive but retir’d the more desirable or  say all nature her self though pure  sinful thought wrought  her so  seeing me she turn’d i follow’d her she what  honour knew and  obsequious majestie approv’d my pleaded reason to  nuptial bowre i led her blushing like  morn all heav’n and happie constellations   houre shed thir selectest influence  earth gave sign  gratulation  each hill joyous  birds fresh gales  gentle aires whisper’d    woods   thir wings flung rose flung odours   spicie shrub disporting till  amorous bird  night sung spousal  bid haste  eevning starr on his hill top  light  bridal lamp thus i have told thee all my state  brought my storie   sum  earthly bliss which i enjoy  must confess feard by us who rather double honour gaine from his surmise prov’d false finde peace within favour  heav’n our witness  th’ event and what  faith love vertue unassaid alone without exterior help rest or ease  mind they sate them down  weep nor onely teares raind  thir eyes but high winds worse within began  rise high passions anger hate mistrust suspicion discord  shook sore thir inward state  mind calme region once and full  peace now tost  turbulent for understanding rul’d not   will heard not her lore both  subjection now to sensual appetite who  beneathe usurping over sovran reason claimd superior sway from thus distemperd brest adam estrang’d  look  alterd stile speech intermitted thus  eve renewd would thou hadst heark’nd  my words  stai’d with me  i besought thee when  strange desire  wandring this unhappie morn i know not whence possessd thee we had then remaind still happie not  now despoild of all our good sham’d naked miserable let none henceforth seek needless cause  approve the faith they owe when earnestly they seek such proof conclude they then begin  faile to whom soon mov’d  touch  blame thus eve what words have past thy lips adam severe imput’st thou   my default or  of wandering  thou call’st it which who knows but might  ill have happ’nd thou being by or  thy self perhaps hadst thou bin there or bere th’ attempt thou couldst not have discernd fraud   serpent speaking   spake no ground  enmitie between us known why hee should mean me ill or seek  harme was i  have never parted  thy side as good have grown there still  liveless rib being  i am why didst not thou  head command me absolutely not  go going into such danger  thou saidst too facil then thou didst not much gainsay nay didst permit approve  fair dismiss hadst thou bin firm  fixt  thy dissent neither had i transgress’d nor thou  mee to whom then first incenst adam repli’d is this  love   recompence of mine  thee ingrateful eve exprest immutable when thou wert lost not i who might have liv’d  joyd immortal bliss yet willingly chose rather death  thee and am i now upbraided   cause of thy transgressing not enough severe it seems  thy restraint what could i more i warn’d thee i admonish’d thee foretold the danger   lurking enemie that lay  wait beyond this had bin force and force upon free will hath here no place but confidence then bore thee on secure either  meet no danger or  finde matter  glorious trial  perhaps i also err’d  overmuch admiring what seemd  thee so perfet  i thought no evil durst attempt thee but i rue that errour now which  become my crime and thou th’ accuser thus  shall befall him who  worth  women overtrusting lets her will rule restraint she  not brook and left  her self if evil thence ensue shee first his weak indulgence  accuse thus they  mutual accusation spent the fruitless hours but neither selfcondemning and  thir vain contest appeer’d no end the end of the eighth book paradise lost book ix meanwhile  hainous  despightfull act of satan done  paradise  how hee   serpent had perverted eve her husband shee  taste  fatall fruit was known  heav’n  what can scape  eye of god allseeing or deceave his heart omniscient who  all things wise  just hinder’d not satan  attempt  minde of man  strength entire  free will arm’d complete  have discover’d  repulst whatever wiles  foe or seeming friend for still they knew  ought  have still remember’d the high injunction not  taste  fruit whoever tempted which they not obeying incurr’d what could they less  penaltie and manifold  sin deserv’d  fall up into heav’n  paradise  hast th’ angelic guards ascended mute  sad for man   his state  this they knew much wondring how  suttle fiend had stoln entrance unseen soon  th’ unwelcome news from earth arriv’d  heaven gate displeas’d all  who heard dim sadness did not spare that time celestial visages yet mixt with pitie violated not thir bliss about  newarriv’d  multitudes th’ ethereal people ran  hear  know how all befell they towards  throne supream accountable made haste  make appear with righteous plea thir utmost vigilance and easily approv’d when  most high eternal father  his secret cloud amidst  thunder utter’d thus his voice assembl’d angels  ye powers return’d from unsuccessful charge  not dismaid nor troubl’d  these tidings   earth which your sincerest care could not prevent foretold so lately what would come  pass when first this tempter cross’d  gulf  hell i told ye then  should prevail  speed on his bad errand man should  seduc’t and flatter’d out  all believing lies against his maker no decree  mine concurring  necessitate his fall or touch  lightest moment  impulse his free will  her own inclining left in eevn scale but fall’n  is  now what rests but   mortal sentence pass on his transgression death denounc’t  day which  presumes already vain  void because not yet inflicted   fear’d by some immediate stroak but soon shall find forbearance no acquittance ere day end justice shall not return  bountie scorn’d but whom send i  judge them whom but thee vicegerent son  thee i have transferr’d all judgement whether  heav’n or earth or hell easie  may  seen  i intend mercie collegue  justice sending thee mans friend his mediator his design’d both ransom  redeemer voluntarie and destin’d man himself  judge man fall’n so spake  father  unfoulding bright toward  right hand his glorie   son blaz’d forth unclouded deitie  full resplendent all his father manifest express’d  thus divinely answer’d milde father eternal thine   decree mine both  heav’n  earth  do thy  supream  thou  mee thy son belov’d mayst ever rest well pleas’d i go  judge on earth these thy transgressors but thou knowst whoever judg’d  worst  mee must light when time shall be  so i undertook before thee  not repenting this obtaine of right  i may mitigate thir doom on me deriv’d yet i shall temper so justice  mercie  may illustrate most them fully satisfied  thee appease attendance none shall need nor train where none are  behold  judgement but  judg’d those two  third best absent  condemn’d convict  flight  rebel  all law conviction   serpent none belongs thus saying  his radiant seat  rose of high collateral glorie him thrones  powers princedoms  dominations ministrant accompanied  heaven gate  whence eden  all  coast  prospect lay down  descended strait  speed  gods time counts not though  swiftest minutes wing’d now   sun  western cadence low from noon  gentle aires due  thir hour to fan  earth now wak’d  usher  the eevning coole when   wrauth more coole came  mild judge  intercessor both to sentence man  voice  god they heard now walking   garden  soft windes brought  thir ears while day declin’d they heard and  his presence hid themselves among the thickest trees both man  wife till god approaching thus  adam call’d aloud where art thou adam wont  joy  meet my coming seen far off i miss thee here not pleas’d thus entertaind  solitude where obvious dutie erewhile appear’d unsaught or come i less conspicuous or what change absents thee or what chance detains come forth he came   him eve more loth though first to offend discount’nanc’t both  discompos’d love  not  thir looks either  god or  each other but apparent guilt and shame  perturbation  despaire anger  obstinacie  hate  guile whence adam faultring long thus answer’d brief i heard thee   garden   thy voice affraid being naked hid my self to whom the gracious judge without revile repli’d my voice thou oft hast heard  hast not fear’d but still rejoyc’t how   now become so dreadful  thee  thou art naked who hath told thee hast thou eaten   tree whereof i gave thee charge thou shouldst not eat to whom thus adam sore beset repli’d o heav’n  evil strait this day i stand before my judge either  undergoe my self  total crime or  accuse my other self  partner  my life whose failing while her faith  me remaines i should conceal  not expose  blame by my complaint but strict necessitie subdues me  calamitous constraint least  my head both sin  punishment however insupportable  all devolv’d though should i hold my peace yet thou wouldst easily detect what i conceale this woman whom thou mad’st   my help and gav’st me  thy perfet gift so good so fit so acceptable so divine that  her hand i could suspect no ill and what she did whatever   self her doing seem’d  justifie  deed shee gave me   tree  i did eate to whom  sovran presence thus repli’d was shee thy god  her thou didst obey before his voice or  shee made thy guide superior or but equal   her thou did’st resigne thy manhood   place wherein god set thee above her made  thee and  thee whose perfection farr excell’d hers  all real dignitie adornd she  indeed  lovely  attract thy love not thy subjection  her gifts were such  under government well seem’d unseemly  beare rule which  thy part and person had’st thou known thy self aright so having said  thus  eve  few say woman what  this which thou hast done to whom sad eve  shame nigh overwhelm’d confessing soon yet not before her judge bold or loquacious thus abasht repli’d the serpent me beguil’d  i did eate which when  lord god heard without delay to judgement  proceeded  th’ accus’d serpent though brute unable  transferre the guilt  him who made him instrument of mischief  polluted   end of his creation justly then accurst as vitiated  nature more  know concern’d not man since  no further knew nor alter’d his offence yet god  last to satan first  sin his doom apply’d though  mysterious terms judg’d  then best and   serpent thus his curse let fall because thou hast done this thou art accurst above all cattel each beast   field upon thy belly groveling thou shalt goe and dust shalt eat all  days  thy life between thee   woman i  put enmitie  between thine  her seed her seed shall bruise thy head thou bruise his heel so spake this oracle then verifi’d when jesus son  mary second eve saw satan fall like lightning down  heav’n prince   aire then rising  his grave spoild principalities  powers triumpht in open shew   ascention bright captivity led captive through  aire the realme  self  satan long usurpt whom  shall tread  last under our feet eevn hee who now foretold his fatal bruise and   woman thus his sentence turn’d thy sorrow i  greatly multiplie by thy conception children thou shalt bring in sorrow forth   thy husbands  thine shall submit hee over thee shall rule on adam last thus judgement  pronounc’d because thou hast heark’nd   voice  thy wife and eaten   tree concerning which i charg’d thee saying thou shalt not eate thereof curs’d   ground  thy sake thou  sorrow shalt eate thereof all  days  thy life thornes also  thistles  shall bring thee forth unbid  thou shalt eate th’ herb  th’ field in  sweat  thy face shalt thou eate bread till thou return unto  ground  thou out   ground wast taken know thy birth for dust thou art  shalt  dust returne so judg’d  man both judge  saviour sent and th’ instant stroke  death denounc’t  day remov’d farr off then pittying how they stood before him naked   aire  now must suffer change disdain’d not  begin thenceforth  forme  servant  assume as when  wash’d his servants feet so now as father  his familie  clad thir nakedness  skins  beasts or slain or   snake  youthful coate repaid and thought not much  cloath his enemies nor hee thir outward onely   skins of beasts but inward nakedness much more opprobrious  his robe  righteousness araying cover’d  his fathers sight to him  swift ascent  up returnd into his blissful bosom reassum’d in glory   old  him appeas’d all though allknowing what had past  man recounted mixing intercession sweet meanwhile ere thus  sin’d  judg’d  earth within  gates  hell sate sin  death in counterview within  gates  now stood open wide belching outrageous flame farr into chaos since  fiend pass’d through sin opening who thus now  death began o son why sit we here each other viewing idlely while satan our great author thrives in other worlds  happier seat provides for us his ofspring deare it cannot  but  success attends him if mishap ere this  had return’d  fury driv’n by his avenger since no place like this can fit his punishment or their revenge methinks i feel new strength within me rise wings growing  dominion giv’n me large beyond this deep whatever drawes me on or sympathie or som connatural force powerful  greatest distance  unite with secret amity things  like kinde by secretest conveyance thou my shade inseparable must  mee along for death  sin no power can separate but least  difficultie  passing back stay his returne perhaps over this gulfe impassable impervious let us try adventrous work yet  thy power  mine not unagreeable  found  path over this maine  hell   new world where satan now prevailes  monument of merit high  all th’ infernal host easing thir passage hence  intercourse or transmigration  thir lot shall lead nor can i miss  way so strongly drawn by this new felt attraction  instinct whom thus  meager shadow answerd soon goe whither fate  inclination strong leads thee i shall not lag behinde nor erre the way thou leading such  sent i draw of carnage prey innumerable  taste the savour  death  all things there  live nor shall i   work thou enterprisest be wanting but afford thee equal aid so saying  delight  snuff’d  smell of mortal change  earth as when  flock of ravenous fowl though many  league remote against  day  battel   field where armies lie encampt come flying lur’d with sent  living carcasses design’d for death  following day  bloodie fight so sented  grim feature  upturn’d his nostril wide into  murkie air sagacious  his quarrey  so farr then both  out hell gates into  waste wide anarchie  chaos damp  dark flew divers   power thir power  great hovering upon  waters what they met solid or slimie   raging sea tost up  down together crowded drove from each side shoaling towards  mouth  hell as when two polar winds blowing adverse upon  cronian sea together drive mountains  ice  stop th’ imagin’d way beyond petsora eastward   rich cathaian coast the aggregated soyle death  his mace petrific cold  dry as   trident smote  fix’t  firm as delos floating once  rest his look bound  gorgonian rigor not  move and  asphaltic slime broad   gate deep   roots  hell  gather’d beach they fasten’d   mole immense great things  small may  compar’d xerxes  libertie  greece  yoke from susa his memnonian palace high came   sea  over hellespont bridging his way europe  asia joyn’d and scourg’d  many  stroak th’ indignant waves now had they brought  work  wondrous art pontifical  ridge  pendent rock over  vext abyss following  track of satan   selfsame place where hee first lighted  his wing  landed safe from out  chaos   outside bare of this round world  pinns  adamant and chains they made all fast too fast they made and durable  now  little space the confines met  empyrean heav’n and  this world    left hand hell with long reach interpos’d three sev’ral wayes in sight  each  these three places led and now thir way  earth they had descri’d to paradise first tending when behold satan  likeness   angel bright betwixt  centaure   scorpion stearing his zenith while  sun  aries rose disguis’d  came but those his children dear thir parent soon discern’d though  disguise hee after eve seduc’t unminded slunk into  wood fast by  changing shape to observe  sequel saw his guileful act by eve though all unweeting seconded upon her husband saw thir shame  sought vain covertures but when  saw descend the son  god  judge them terrifi’d hee fled not hoping  escape but shun the present fearing guiltie what his wrauth might suddenly inflict  past return’d by night  listning where  hapless paire sate  thir sad discourse  various plaint thence gatherd his own doom which understood not instant but  future time with joy and tidings fraught  hell  now return’d and   brink  chaos neer  foot of this new wondrous pontifice unhop’t met who  meet him came his ofspring dear great joy   thir meeting   sight of  stupendious bridge his joy encreas’d long hee admiring stood till sin his faire inchanting daughter thus  silence broke o parent these  thy magnific deeds thy trophies which thou view’st  not thine own thou art thir author  prime architect for i no sooner  my heart divin’d my heart which   secret harmonie still moves  thine joyn’d  connexion sweet that thou  earth hadst prosper’d which thy looks now also evidence but straight i felt though distant  thee worlds between yet felt that i must after thee  this thy son such fatal consequence unites us three hell could no longer hold us  her bounds nor this unvoyageable gulf obscure detain  following thy illustrious track thou hast atchiev’d our libertie confin’d within hell gates till now thou us impow’rd to fortifie thus farr  overlay with this portentous bridge  dark abyss thine now  all this world thy vertue hath won what thy hands builded not thy wisdom gain’d with odds what warr hath lost  fully aveng’d our foile  heav’n here thou shalt monarch reign there didst not there let him still victor sway as battel hath adjudg’d  this new world retiring  his own doom alienated and henceforth monarchie  thee divide of all things parted  th’ empyreal bounds his quadrature  thy orbicular world or trie thee now more dang’rous  his throne whom thus  prince  darkness answerd glad fair daughter  thou son  grandchild both high proof ye now have giv’n    race of satan for i glorie   name antagonist  heav’ns almightie king amply have merited  me  all th’ infernal empire  so neer heav’ns dore triumphal  triumphal act have met mine  this glorious work  made one realm hell  this world one realm one continent of easie thoroughfare therefore while i descend through darkness  your rode  ease to my associate powers them  acquaint with these successes   them rejoyce you two this way among those numerous orbs all yours right down  paradise descend there dwell  reign  bliss thence   earth dominion exercise    aire chiefly  man sole lord  all declar’d him first make sure your thrall  lastly kill my substitutes i send ye  create plenipotent  earth  matchless might issuing  mee  your joynt vigor now my hold  this new kingdom all depends through sin  death expos’d  my exploit if your joynt power prevaile th’ affaires  hell no detriment need feare goe   strong so saying  dismiss’d them they  speed thir course through thickest constellations held spreading thir bane  blasted starrs lookt wan and planets planetstrook real eclips then sufferd th’ other way satan went down the causey  hell gate  either side disparted chaos over built exclaimd and  rebounding surge  barrs assaild that scorn’d his indignation through citie  proud seate of lucifer so  allusion calld of  bright starr  satan paragond there kept thir watch  legions while  grand in council sate sollicitous what chance might intercept thir emperour sent so hee departing gave command  they observ’d as when  tartar  his russian foe by astracan over  snowie plaines retires or bactrian sophi   hornes of turkish crescent leaves all waste beyond the realme  aladule  his retreate to tauris or casbeen so these  late heav’nbanisht host left desert utmost hell many  dark league reduc’t  careful watch round thir metropolis  now expecting each hour their great adventurer   search of forrein worlds  through  midst unmarkt in shew plebeian angel militant of lowest order past    dore of  plutonian hall invisible ascended his high throne which under state of richest texture spred  th’ upper end was plac’t  regal lustre down  while he sate  round about him saw unseen at last    cloud his fulgent head and shape starr bright appeer’d or brighter clad with what permissive glory since his fall was left him or false glitter all amaz’d at  so sudden blaze  stygian throng bent thir aspect  whom they wish’d beheld thir mighty chief returnd loud  th’ acclaime forth rush’d  haste  great consulting peers rais’d  thir dark divan   like joy congratulant approach’d him who  hand silence   these words attention won thrones dominations princedoms vertues powers for  possession such not onely  right i call ye  declare ye now returnd successful beyond hope  lead ye forth triumphant out  this infernal pit abominable accurst  house  woe and dungeon  our tyrant now possess as lords  spacious world  our native heaven little inferiour  my adventure hard with peril great atchiev’d long   tell what i have don what sufferd  what paine voyag’d  unreal vast unbounded deep of horrible confusion over which by sin  death  broad way now  pav’d to expedite your glorious march but i toild out my uncouth passage forc’t  ride th’ untractable abysse plung’d   womb of unoriginal night  chaos wilde that jealous  thir secrets fiercely oppos’d my journey strange  clamorous uproare protesting fate supreame thence how i found the new created world which fame  heav’n long had foretold  fabrick wonderful of absolute perfection therein man plac’t   paradise  our exile made happie him  fraud i have seduc’d from his creator   more  increase your wonder   apple  thereat offended worth your laughter hath giv’n up both his beloved man  all his world to sin  death  prey  so  us without our hazard labour or allarme to range in   dwell  over man to rule  over all  should have rul’d true is mee also  hath judg’d or rather mee not but  brute serpent  whose shape man i deceav’d  which  mee belongs is enmity which   put between mee  mankinde i am  bruise his heel his seed when  not set shall bruise my head a world who would not purchase   bruise or much more grievous pain ye have th’ account of my performance what remaines ye gods but up  enter now into full bliss so having said  while  stood expecting thir universal shout  high applause to fill his eare when contrary  hears on all sides  innumerable tongues a dismal universal hiss  sound of public scorn  wonderd but not long had leasure wondring  himself now more his visage drawn  felt  sharp  spare his armes clung  his ribs his leggs entwining each other till supplanted down  fell a monstrous serpent  his belly prone reluctant but  vaine  greater power now rul’d him punisht   shape  sin’d according  his doom  would have spoke but hiss  hiss returnd  forked tongue to forked tongue  now  all transform’d alike  serpents all  accessories to his bold riot dreadful   din of hissing through  hall thick swarming now with complicated monsters head  taile scorpion  asp  amphisbaena dire cerastes hornd hydrus  ellops drear and dipsas not so thick swarm’d once  soil bedropt  blood  gorgon or  isle ophiusa but still greatest hee  midst now dragon grown larger then whom  sun ingenderd   pythian vale  slime huge python  his power no less  seem’d above  rest still  retain they all him follow’d issuing forth  th’ open field where all yet left   revolted rout heav’nfall’n  station stood or just array sublime  expectation when  see in triumph issuing forth thir glorious chief they saw but other sight instead  crowd of ugly serpents horror  them fell and horrid sympathie  what they saw they felt themselvs now changing down thir arms down fell both spear  shield down they  fast and  dire hiss renew’d   dire form catcht  contagion like  punishment as  thir crime thus  th’ applause they meant turnd  exploding hiss triumph  shame cast  themselves  thir own mouths there stood a grove hard by sprung up  this thir change his  who reigns above  aggravate thir penance laden  fair fruit like  vvhich grew  paradise  bait  eve us’d   tempter   prospect strange thir earnest eyes they fix’d imagining for one forbidden tree  multitude now ris’n  work them furder woe or shame yet parcht  scalding thurst  hunger fierce though  delude them sent could not abstain but  they rould  heaps  up  trees climbing sat thicker then  snakie locks that curld megaera greedily they pluck’d the frutage fair  sight like  which grew neer  bituminous lake where sodom flam’d this more delusive not  touch but taste deceav’d they fondly thinking  allay thir appetite  gust instead  fruit chewd bitter ashes which th’ offended taste vvith spattering noise rejected oft they assayd hunger  thirst constraining drugd  oft vvith hatefullest disrelish writh’d thir jaws vvith foot  cinders fill’d so oft they fell into  same illusion not  man whom they triumph’d once lapst thus  they plagu’d and worn  famin long  ceasless hiss till thir lost shape permitted they resum’d yearly enjoynd some say  undergo this annual humbling certain number’d days to dash thir pride  joy  man seduc’t however some tradition they dispers’d among  heathen  thir purchase got and fabl’d how  serpent whom they calld ophion  eurynome  wide encroaching eve perhaps had first  rule of high olympus thence  saturn driv’n and ops ere yet dictaean jove  born mean while  paradise  hellish pair too soon arriv’d sin there  power before once actual now  body   dwell habitual habitant behind her death close following pace  pace not mounted yet on his pale horse  whom sin thus began second  satan sprung all conquering death what thinkst thou  our empire now though earnd with travail difficult not better farr then stil  hels dark threshold  have sate watch unnam’d undreaded  thy self half starv’d whom thus  sinborn monster answerd soon to mee who  eternal famin pine alike  hell or paradise or heaven there best where most  ravin i may meet which here though plenteous all too little seems to stuff this maw this vast unhidebound corps to whom th’ incestuous mother thus repli’d thou therefore  these herbs  fruits  flours feed first  each beast next  fish  fowle no homely morsels  whatever thing the sithe  time mowes down devour unspar’d till i  man residing through  race his thoughts his looks words actions all infect and season him thy last  sweetest prey this said they both betook them several wayes both  destroy or unimmortal make all kinds   destruction  mature sooner or later which th’ almightie seeing from his transcendent seat  saints among to those bright orders utterd thus his voice see  what heat these dogs  hell advance to waste  havoc yonder vvorld which i so fair  good created  had still kept   state had not  folly  man let  these wastful furies who impute folly  mee so doth  prince  hell and his adherents   so much ease i suffer them  enter  possess a place so heav’nly  conniving seem to gratifie my scornful enemies that laugh  if transported  some fit of passion i  them had quitted all at random yeilded up  their misrule and know not  i call’d  drew them thither my hellhounds  lick up  draff  filth which mans polluting sin  taint hath shed on what  pure till cramm’d  gorg’d nigh burst with suckt  glutted offal  one fling of thy victorious arm wellpleasing son both sin  death  yawning grave  last through chaos hurld obstruct  mouth  hell for ever  seal up his ravenous jawes then heav’n  earth renewd shall  made pure to sanctitie  shall receive no staine till then  curse pronounc’t  both precedes hee ended   heav’nly audience loud sung halleluia   sound  seas through multitude  sung just  thy ways righteous  thy decrees  all thy works who can extenuate thee next   son destin’d restorer  mankind  whom new heav’n  earth shall   ages rise or down  heav’n descend such  thir song while  creator calling forth  name his mightie angels gave them several charge as sorted best  present things the sun had first his precept so  move so shine as might affect  earth  cold  heat scarce tollerable    north  call decrepit winter   south  bring solstitial summers heat to  blanc moone her office they prescrib’d  th’ other five thir planetarie motions  aspects in sextile square  trine  opposite of noxious efficacie  when  joyne in synod unbenigne  taught  fixt thir influence malignant when  showre which  them rising   sun or falling should prove tempestuous to  winds they set thir corners when  bluster  confound sea aire  shoar  thunder when  rowle with terror through  dark aereal hall some say  bid his angels turne ascanse the poles  earth twice ten degrees  more from  suns axle they  labour push’d oblique  centric globe som say  sun was bid turn reines  th’ equinoctial rode like distant breadth  taurus   seav’n atlantick sisters   spartan twins up   tropic crab thence down amaine by leo   virgin   scales as deep  capricorne  bring  change of seasons  each clime else had  spring perpetual smil’d  earth  vernant flours equal  days  nights except  those beyond  polar circles  them day had unbenighted shon while  low sun to recompence his distance  thir sight had rounded still th’ horizon  not known or east or west which had forbid  snow from cold estotiland  south  farr beneath magellan at  tasted fruit the sun   thyestean banquet turn’d his course intended else how had  world inhabited though sinless more then now avoided pinching cold  scorching heate these changes   heav’ns though slow produc’d like change  sea  land sideral blast vapour  mist  exhalation hot corrupt  pestilent now   north of norumbega   samoed shoar bursting daughter  sin among th’ irrational death introduc’d through fierce antipathie beast now  beast gan war  fowle  fowle and fish  fish  graze  herb all leaving devourd each other nor stood much  awe of promis’d clearer sight had bred then purg’d  euphrasie  rue the visual nerve   had much  see and   vvell  life three drops instill’d so deep  power  these ingredients pierc’d eevn   inmost seat  mental sight that adam now enforc’t  close his eyes sunk down  all his spirits became intranst but him  gentle angel   hand soon rais’d  his attention thus recall’d adam now ope thine eyes  first behold th’ effects which thy original crime hath wrought in some  spring  thee who never touch’d th’ excepted tree nor   snake conspir’d nor sinn’d thy sin yet   sin derive corruption  bring forth more violent deeds his eyes  op’nd  beheld  field part arable  tilth whereon  sheaves new reapt  other part sheepwalks  foulds ith’ midst  altar   landmark stood rustic  grassie sord thither anon a sweatie reaper  his tillage brought first fruits  green eare   yellow sheaf uncull’d  came  hand  shepherd next more meek came   firstlings  his flock choicest  best then sacrificing laid the inwards  thir fat  incense strew’d on  cleft wood  all due rites perform’d his offring soon propitious fire  heav’n consum’d  nimble glance  grateful steame the others not  his  not sincere whereat hee inlie rag’d   they talk’d smote him into  midriff   stone that beat out life  fell  deadly pale groand out his soul  gushing bloud effus’d much   sight  adam  his heart dismai’d  thus  haste  th’ angel cri’d o teacher some great mischief hath befall’n to  meek man who well had sacrific’d is pietie thus  pure devotion paid t’ whom michael thus hee also mov’d repli’d these two  brethren adam   come out  thy loyns th’ unjust  just hath slain for envie  his brothers offering found from heav’n acceptance but  bloodie fact will  aveng’d  th’ others faith approv’d loose no reward though here thou see him die rowling  dust  gore to which our sire alas both   deed    cause but have i now seen death is this  way i must return  native dust o sight of terrour foul  ugly  behold horrid  think how horrible  feel to whom thus michael death thou hast seen in his first shape  man but many shapes of death  many   wayes  lead to his grim cave all dismal yet  sense more terrible  th’ entrance then within some  thou saw’st  violent stroke shall die by fire flood famin  intemperance more in meats  drinks which   earth shal bring diseases dire  which  monstrous crew before thee shall appear  thou mayst know what miserie th’ inabstinence  eve shall bring  men immediately  place before his eyes appeard sad noysom dark a lazarhouse  seemd wherein  laid numbers  all diseas’d all maladies of gastly spasm or racking torture qualmes of heartsick agonie all feavorous kinds convulsions epilepsies fierce catarrhs intestin stone  ulcer colic pangs dropsies  asthma’s  jointracking rheums dire   tossing deep  groans despair tended  sick busiest  couch  couch and over them triumphant death his dart shook but delaid  strike though oft invok’t with vows  thir chief good  final hope sight so deform what heart  rock could long drieey’d behold adam could not but wept though not  woman born compassion quell’d his best  man  gave him up  tears a space till firmer thoughts restraind excess and scarce recovering words his plaint renew’d o miserable mankind  what fall degraded  what wretched state reserv’d better end heer unborn why  life giv’n to  thus wrested  us rather why obtruded  us thus who if we knew what we receive would either not accept life offer’d or soon beg  lay  down glad   so dismist  peace can thus th’ image  god  man created once so goodly  erect though faultie since to such unsightly sufferings  debas’t under inhuman pains why should not man retaining still divine similitude in part  such deformities  free and  his makers image sake exempt thir makers image answerd michael then forsook them when themselves they villifi’d to serve ungovern’d appetite  took his image whom they serv’d  brutish vice inductive mainly   sin  eve therefore so abject  thir punishment disfiguring not gods likeness but thir own or if his likeness  themselves defac’t while they pervert pure natures healthful rules to loathsom sickness worthily since they gods image did not reverence  themselves i yeild  just said adam  submit but  there yet no other way besides these painful passages how we may come to death  mix  our connatural dust there is said michael if thou well observe the rule  not too much  temperance taught in what thou eatst  drinkst seeking  thence due nourishment not gluttonous delight till many years over thy head return so maist thou live till like ripe fruit thou drop into thy mothers lap or   ease gatherd not harshly pluckt  death mature this  old age but then thou must outlive thy youth thy strength thy beauty which  change to witherd weak  gray thy senses then obtuse all taste  pleasure must forgoe to what thou hast    aire  youth hopeful  cheerful  thy blood  reigne a melancholly damp  cold  dry to waigh thy spirits down  last consume the balme  life to whom our ancestor henceforth i flie not death nor would prolong life much bent rather how i may  quit fairest  easiest  this combrous charge which i must keep till my appointed day of rendring up michael  him repli’d nor love thy life nor hate but what thou livst live well how long or short permit  heav’n and now prepare thee  another sight he lookd  saw  spacious plaine whereon were tents  various hue  some  herds of cattel grazing others whence  sound of instruments  made melodious chime was heard  harp  organ  who moovd thir stops  chords  seen his volant touch instinct men they seemd  all thir study bent to worship god aright  know his works not hid nor those things lost which might preserve freedom  peace  men they   plain long had not walkt when   tents behold a beavie  fair women richly gay in gems  wanton dress   harp they sung soft amorous ditties   dance came on the men though grave ey’d them  let thir eyes rove without rein till   amorous net fast caught they lik’d  each his liking chose and now  love they treat till th’ eevning star loves harbinger appeerd then all  heat they light  nuptial torch  bid invoke hymen then first  marriage rites invok’t with feast  musick all  tents resound such happy interview  fair event of love  youth not lost songs garlands flours and charming symphonies attach’d  heart of adam soon enclin’d  admit delight the bent  nature which  thus express’d true opener  mine eyes prime angel blest much better seems this vision  more hope of peaceful dayes portends then those two past those   hate  death or pain much worse here nature seems fulfilld  all her ends to whom thus michael judg not what  best by pleasure though  nature seeming meet created  thou art  nobler end holie  pure conformitie divine those tents these deaths ministers not men who thus deal death inhumanly  men  multiply ten thousand fould  sin  him who slew his brother   whom such massacher make they but  thir brethren men  men but who   just man whom had not heav’n rescu’d had  his righteousness bin lost to whom thus michael these   product of those illmated marriages thou saw’st where good  bad  matcht who  themselves abhor  joyn dayes lot anough  bear those now   dispenst the burd’n  many ages  me light at once  my foreknowledge gaining birth abortive  torment me ere thir being with thought  they must be let no man seek whom thus michael those whom last thou sawst in triumph  luxurious wealth  they first seen  acts  prowess eminent and great exploits but  true vertu void who having spilt much blood  don much waste subduing nations  achievd thereby fame   world high titles  rich prey shall change thir course  pleasure ease  sloth surfet  lust till wantonness  pride raise out  friendship hostil deeds  peace the things new both heav’n  earth wherein  just shall dwell thus thou hast seen one world begin  end and man    second stock proceed much thou hast yet  see but i perceave thy mortal sight  faile objects his game with warr  hostile snare such  refuse subjection  his empire tyrannous a mightie hunter thence  shall  styl’d before  lord   despite  heav’n or  heav’n claming second sovrantie and  rebellion gurge boiles out  under ground  mouth  hell of brick    stuff they cast  build a citie  towre whose top may reach  heav’n and get themselves  name least far disperst in foraign lands thir memorie  lost regardless whether good or evil fame but god who oft descends  visit men unseen  through thir habitations walks to mark thir doings them beholding soon comes down  see thir citie ere  tower confusion nam’d whereto thus adam fatherly displeas’d o execrable son so  aspire above his brethren  himself affirming authoritie usurpt  god not giv’n he gave us onely over beast fish fowl dominion absolute  right we hold by his donation but man over men he made not lord such title  himself reserving human left  human free but this usurper his encroachment proud stayes not  man  god his tower intends siege  defiance wretched man what food will  convey up thither  sustain himself  his rash armie where thin aire above  clouds  pine his entrails gross and famish him  breath if not  bread to alwayes  right reason dwells twinn’d   her hath no dividual being reason  man obscur’d or not obeyd immediately inordinate desires and upstart passions catch  government from reason   servitude reduce man till then free therefore since hee permits within himself unworthie powers  reign over free reason god  judgement just subjects him  without  violent lords who oft  undeservedly enthrall his outward freedom tyrannie must be though   tyrant thereby no excuse yet somtimes nations  decline so low from vertue which  reason  no wrong but justice  some fatal curse annext deprives them  thir outward libertie thir inward lost witness th’ irreverent son of him who built  ark who   shame don  his father heard this heavie curse servant  servants  his vitious race thus  this latter   former graine a darksom cloud  locusts swarming down must eat    ground leave nothing green darkness must overshadow all his bounds palpable darkness  blot out three dayes last  one midnight stroke all  firstborn of egypt must lie dead thus  ten wounds this riverdragon tam’d  length submits to let his sojourners depart  oft humbles his stubborn heart but still  ice more hard’nd after thaw till  his rage pursuing whom  late dismissd  sea swallows him  his host but them lets pass as  drie land between two christal walls aw’d   rod  moses so  stand divided till his rescu’d gain thir shoar such wondrous power god  his saint  lend though present  his angel who shall goe before them   cloud  pillar  fire to guide them  thir journey  remove behinde them while th’ obdurat king pursues all night   pursue but his approach darkness defends between till morning watch then through  firey pillar   cloud god looking forth  trouble all his host and craze thir chariot wheels when  command moses once more his potent rod extends over  sea  sea his rod obeys on thir imbattelld ranks  waves return and overwhelm thir warr  race elect safe towards canaan   shoar advance through  wilde desert not mount  sinai whose gray top shall tremble  descending  himself in thunder lightning  loud trumpets sound ordaine them lawes part such  appertaine to civil justice part religious rites of sacrifice informing them  types and shadowes   destind seed  bruise the serpent  what meanes  shall achieve mankinds deliverance but  voice  god to mortal eare  dreadful they beseech that moses might report sent  heav’n enlightner  my darkness gracious things thou hast reveald those chiefly which concerne just abraham  his seed now first i finde mine eyes true op’ning  my heart much eas’d erwhile perplext  thoughts what would becom of mee  all mankind but now i see his day  whom all nations shall  blest favour unmerited  me who sought forbidd’n knowledge  forbidd’n means this yet i apprehend not why  those among whom god  deigne  dwell  earth so many  so various laws  giv’n so many laws argue so many sins among them how can god  such reside to whom thus michael doubt not but  sin will reign among them   thee begot and therefore  law given them  evince thir natural pravitie  stirring up sin against law  fight  when they see law can discover sin but not remove save  those shadowie expiations weak the bloud  bulls  goats they may conclude some bloud more precious must  paid  man just  unjust   such righteousness to them  faith imputed they may finde justification towards god  peace of conscience which  law  ceremonies cannot appease nor man  moral part perform  not performing cannot live so law appears imperfet  but giv’n with purpose  resign them  full time up   better cov’nant disciplin’d from shadowie types  truth  flesh  spirit from imposition  strict laws  free acceptance  large grace  servil fear to filial works  law  works  faith and therefore shall not moses though  god highly belov’d being but  minister of law his people into canaan lead but joshua whom  gentiles jesus call his name  office bearing who shall quell the adversarie serpent  bring back through  worlds wilderness long wanderd man safe  eternal paradise  rest meanwhile they  thir earthly canaan plac’t long time shall dwell  prosper but when sins national interrupt thir public peace provoking god  raise them enemies from whom  oft  saves them penitent by judges first then under kings  whom the second both  pietie renownd and puissant deeds  promise shall receive irrevocable  his regal throne for ever shall endure  like shall sing all prophecie that   royal stock of david so i name this king shall rise a son  womans seed  thee foretold foretold  abraham   whom shall trust all nations   kings foretold  kings the last   his reign shall  no end but first  long succession must ensue and his next son  wealth  wisdom fam’d the clouded ark  god till then  tents wandring shall   glorious temple enshrine such follow him  shall  registerd part good part bad  bad  longer scrowle whose foul idolatries  other faults heapt   popular summe  so incense god   leave them  expose thir land thir citie his temple  his holy ark with all his sacred things  scorn  prey to  proud citie whose high walls thou saw’st left  confusion babylon thence call’d there  captivitie  lets them dwell the space  seventie years then brings them back remembring mercie  his cov’nant sworn to david stablisht   dayes  heav’n returnd  babylon  leave  kings thir lords whom god dispos’d  house  god they first reedifie    while in mean estate live moderate till grown in wealth  multitude factious they grow but first among  priests dissension springs men who attend  altar  should most endeavour peace thir strife pollution brings upon  temple  self  last they seise the scepter  regard not davids sons then loose    stranger   true anointed king messiah might  born barr’d  his right yet  his birth  starr unseen before  heav’n proclaims him com and guides  eastern sages who enquire his place  offer incense myrrh  gold his place  birth  solemn angel tells to simple shepherds keeping watch  night they gladly thither haste    quire of squadrond angels hear his carol sung a virgin  his mother but his sire the power   most high  shall ascend the throne hereditarie  bound his reign with earths wide bounds his glory   heav’ns he ceas’d discerning adam  such joy surcharg’d  had like grief bin dew’d  tears without  vent  words which these  breathd o prophet  glad tidings finisher of utmost hope now clear i understand what oft my steddiest thoughts have searcht  vain why our great expectation should  call’d the seed  woman virgin mother haile high   love  heav’n yet  my loynes thou shalt proceed   thy womb  son of god most high so god  man unites needs must  serpent now his capital bruise expect  mortal paine say where  when thir fight what stroke shall bruise  victors heel to whom thus michael dream not  thir fight as   duel or  local wounds of head or heel not therefore joynes  son manhood  godhead  more strength  foil thy enemie nor so  overcome satan whose fall  heav’n  deadlier bruise disabl’d not  give thee thy deaths wound which hee who comes thy saviour shall recure not  destroying satan but his works in thee   thy seed nor can this be but  fulfilling  which thou didst want obedience   law  god impos’d on penaltie  death  suffering death the penaltie  thy transgression due and due  theirs which out  thine  grow so onely can high justice rest appaid the law  god exact  shall fulfill both  obedience   love though love alone fulfill  law thy punishment he shall endure  coming   flesh to  reproachful life  cursed death proclaiming life  all who shall believe in his redemption   his obedience imputed becomes theirs  faith his merits to save them not thir own though legal works for this  shall live hated  blasphem’d seis’d   force judg’d   death condemnd a shameful  accurst naild   cross by his own nation slaine  bringing life but   cross  nailes thy enemies the law   against thee   sins of all mankinde  him there crucifi’d never  hurt them more who rightly trust in this his satisfaction so  dies but soon revives death over him no power shall long usurp ere  third dawning light returne  starres  morn shall see him rise out  his grave fresh   dawning light thy ransom paid which man  death redeems his death  man  many  offerd life neglect not   benefit imbrace by faith not void  works this godlike act annuls thy doom  death thou shouldst have dy’d in sin  ever lost  life this act shall bruise  head  satan crush his strength defeating sin  death his two maine armes and fix farr deeper  his head thir stings then temporal death shall bruise  victors heel or theirs whom  redeems  death like sleep a gentle wafting  immortal life nor after resurrection shall  stay longer  earth then certaine times  appeer to his disciples men who  his life still follow’d him  them shall leave  charge to teach all nations what  him they learn’d and his salvation them who shall beleeve baptizing   profluent streame  signe of washing them  guilt  sin  life pure   mind prepar’d if so befall for death like  which  redeemer dy’d all nations they shall teach    day not onely   sons  abrahams loines salvation shall  preacht but   sons of abrahams faith wherever through  world so  his seed all nations shall  blest then   heav’n  heav’ns  shall ascend with victory triumphing through  aire over his foes  thine there shall surprise the serpent prince  aire  drag  chaines through all his realme  there confounded leave then enter into glory  resume his seat  gods right hand exalted high above all names  heav’n  thence shall come when this worlds dissolution shall  ripe with glory  power  judge both quick  dead to judge th’ unfaithful dead but  reward his faithful  receave them into bliss whether  heav’n or earth  then  earth shall all  paradise far happier place then this  eden  far happier daies so spake th’ archangel michael then paus’d as   worlds great period  our sire replete  joy  wonder thus repli’d o goodness infinite goodness immense that all this good  evil shall produce and evil turn  good more wonderful then  which  creation first brought forth light out  darkness full  doubt i stand whether i should repent me now  sin by mee done  occasiond or rejoyce much more  much more good thereof shall spring to god more glory more good   men from god  over wrauth grace shall abound but say if our deliverer up  heav’n must reascend what  betide  few his faithful left among th’ unfaithful herd the enemies  truth who then shall guide his people who defend  they not deale wors  his followers then  him they dealt be sure they will said th’ angel but  heav’n hee  his own  comforter  send the promise   father who shall dwell his spirit within them   law  faith working through love upon thir hearts shall write to guide them  all truth  also arme with spiritual armour able  resist satans assaults  quench his fierie darts what man can do against them not affraid though   death against such cruelties with inward consolations recompenc’t and oft supported so  shall amaze thir proudest persecuters   spirit powrd first  his apostles whom  sends to evangelize  nations then  all baptiz’d shall them  wondrous gifts endue to speak all tongues  do all miracles as did thir lord before them thus they win great numbers  each nation  receave with joy  tidings brought  heav’n  length thir ministry perform’d  race well run thir doctrine  thir story written left they die but  thir room  they forewarne wolves shall succeed  teachers grievous wolves who all  sacred mysteries  heav’n to thir own vile advantages shall turne of lucre  ambition   truth with superstitions  traditions taint left onely  those written records pure though not but   spirit understood then shall they seek  avail themselves  names places  titles   these  joine secular power though feigning still  act by spiritual  themselves appropriating the spirit  god promisd alike  giv’n to all beleevers    pretense spiritual lawes  carnal power shall force on every conscience laws which none shall finde left them inrould or what  spirit within shall   heart engrave what  they then but force  spirit  grace  self  binde his consort libertie what but unbuild his living temples built  faith  stand thir own faith not anothers   earth who against faith  conscience can  heard infallible yet many  presume whence heavie persecution shall arise on all who   worship persevere of spirit  truth  rest farr greater part will deem  outward rites  specious formes religion satisfi’d truth shall retire bestuck  slandrous darts  works  faith rarely  found so shall  world goe on to good malignant  bad men benigne under her own waight groaning till  day appeer  respiration   just and vengeance   wicked  return of him so lately promis’d  thy aid the womans seed obscurely then foretold now amplier known thy saviour  thy lord last   clouds  heav’n   reveald in glory   father  dissolve satan  his perverted world then raise from  conflagrant mass purg’d  refin’d new heav’ns new earth ages  endless date founded  righteousness  peace  love to bring forth fruits joy  eternal bliss he ended  thus adam last reply’d how soon hath thy prediction seer blest measur’d this transient world  race  time till time stand fixt beyond  all abyss eternitie whose end no eye can reach greatly instructed i shall hence depart greatly  peace  thought  have my fill of knowledge what this vessel can containe beyond which  my folly  aspire henceforth i learne   obey  best and love  feare  onely god  walk as  his presence ever  observe his providence   him sole depend merciful over all his works  good still overcoming evil   small accomplishing great things  things deemd weak subverting worldly strong  worldly wise by simply meek  suffering  truths sake is fortitude  highest victorie and   faithful death  gate  life taught this  his example whom i now acknowledge my redeemer ever blest to whom thus also th’ angel last repli’d this having learnt thou hast attaind  summe of wisdom hope no higher though all  starrs thou knewst  name  all th’ ethereal powers all secrets   deep all natures works or works  god  heav’n air earth or sea and all  riches  this world enjoydst and all  rule one empire onely add deeds  thy knowledge answerable add faith add vertue patience temperance add love by name  come call’d charitie  soul of all  rest then wilt thou not  loath to leave this paradise but shalt possess a paradise within thee happier farr let us descend now therefore  this top of speculation   hour precise exacts our parting hence  see  guards by mee encampt  yonder hill expect thir motion  whose front  flaming sword in signal  remove waves fiercely round we may no longer stay go waken eve her also i  gentle dreams have calm’d portending good  all her spirits compos’d to meek submission thou  season fit let her  thee partake what thou hast heard chiefly what may concern her faith  know the great deliverance  her seed  come for   womans seed  all mankind that ye may live which   many dayes both  one faith unanimous though sad with cause  evils past yet much more cheer’d with meditation   happie end he ended  they both descend  hill descended adam   bowre where eve lay sleeping ran before but found her wak’t and thus  words not sad she him receav’d whence thou returnst  whither wentst i know for god  also  sleep  dreams advise which  hath sent propitious some great good presaging since  sorrow  hearts distress vvearied i fell asleep but now lead on in mee  no delay  thee  goe is  stay here without thee here  stay is  go hence unwilling thou  mee art all things under heav’n all places thou vvho  my wilful crime art banisht hence this further consolation yet secure i carry hence though all  mee  lost such favour i unworthie am voutsaft by mee  promis’d seed shall all restore so spake our mother eve  adam heard vvell pleas’d but answer’d not  now too nigh th’ archangel stood    other hill to thir fixt station all  bright array the cherubim descended   ground gliding meteorous  ev’ning mist ris’n   river o’re  marish glides and gathers ground fast   labourers heel homeward returning high  front advanc’t the brandisht sword  god before them blaz’d fierce   comet which  torrid heat and vapour   libyan air adust began  parch  temperate clime whereat in either hand  hastning angel caught our lingring parents   th’ eastern gate let them direct  down  cliff  fast to  subjected plaine then disappeer’d they looking back all th’ eastern side beheld of paradise so late thir happie seat wav’d over   flaming brand  gate with dreadful faces throng’d  fierie armes som natural tears they drop’d but wip’d them soon the world  all before them where  choose thir place  rest  providence thir guide they hand  hand  wandring steps  slow through eden took thir solitarie way the end  end of the project gutenberg ebook paradise lost  updated editions  replace  previous onethe old editions   renamed creating
